France and Czechoslovakia Reach Agreement: The Foundation of the League of Nations Will Not Be Shaken; Disarmament Resolved in Geneva; Economic Cooperation Maintained in Central Europe; Czech Foreign Minister Departs Paris for Home Today 46

(Paris) When French Foreign Minister Pongou and Czech Foreign Minister Dr. Piniš spoke today, they reached a complete agreement on the three major issues of League of Nations reform, disarmament, and the aftermath of Central European economies. After the two foreign ministers spoke, they released a statement to the press. Pongou stated that Dr. Piniš's official visit to Paris was not intended to oppose any policy or any country, but to further international cooperation. What both sides resolved was to support the League of Nations without shaking it in the slightest, believing that improving the League's methods of doing things is more beneficial than reforming its organization. As for disarmament talks, no matter what progress is made in various aspects, the final result will be produced in Geneva. France and Czechoslovakia believe that economic cooperation in Central Europe can be achieved. Dr. Piniš said in this regard that Czechoslovakia's negotiations with Austria on this matter are currently underway and are expected to be successful. (16th Reuters Dispatch)

(Paris) Today, President Lebrun hosted Czech Foreign Minister Belles for lunch. After the meal, Belles spoke with Prime Minister Xu Dang, and then went to the French Academy's welcome ceremony. After the event, Belles returned to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. In front of Belles, Foreign Minister Pongou received journalists and issued a declaration, stating that since the Czech Foreign Minister was also present at this press conference, it showed that the two countries' opinions were completely consistent. Both sides had lengthy talks and conducted thorough research on international issues. Pongou also said that the thoughts he expressed when he spoke with Belles were the same as those of Prime Minister Xu Dang. Pongou also stated that the Czech Foreign Minister's visit to France had no other intention than to cooperate with France. The first issue studied by both sides was the League of Nations meeting and the issue of League of Nations reform that may be proposed. Both sides believed that the best way to devote ourselves to the League of Nations was to express our unwavering trust in the League of Nations. If our international peace organization is still very weak, if we listen to the League of Nations reducing its strength or allow it to be eliminated, then this weak peace organization will also collapse. Pongou also said that although the League of Nations cannot be considered permanently immutable, we can improve it, but if its fundamental principles are shaken, the League of Nations' reason for existence will be lost. Therefore, it is more beneficial to reform its working methods than to propose reorganizing the League of Nations. Regarding the issue of disarmament, Pongou and Belles agreed to declare that the final solution to this matter should be sought in Geneva. Pongou also said that the Czech Foreign Minister had told him that Czechoslovakia and Austria had hopes of success in their negotiations on economic issues between the two countries, and that the economic cooperation among the countries of the Little Entente was very close. At this point, Belles told reporters that he agreed with Pongou's statement and recalled the past cooperation between France and Czechoslovakia, saying that the two countries had friendly relations and that he and Pongou were old friends, so it was very convenient for them to discuss matters. Pongou's statement was a sign that the two foreign ministers' negotiations had come to an end, and it was also the last expression during Belles' official visit to France. Belles is scheduled to leave for the Czech capital next Monday. (16th Havas Dispatch)

Germany's Armament Demands: Reactions in London; British Ambassador to Return to Berlin to Report 47

(London) German Prime Minister Hitler's proposals to French Ambassador Ponset regarding disarmament matters have created a new situation. British Ambassador to Germany Fife will bring these proposals to London at the end of this week to discuss them with Foreign Secretary Simon. According to diplomatic reporters, the main points are as follows: (1) Germany may increase its national defense force from 100,000 to 300,000, and its long-term military service will be changed to short-term military service, but Germany is willing to sign non-aggression pacts with various countries. (2) Germany may take various reasonable steps to eliminate nationalistic militarism, but other countries must also take such actions. (3) Germany, like other countries, also agrees to a system of inspecting armaments, but this system is not convenient to implement when reorganizing the national defense force. (4) Germany is in favor of gradually abolishing heavy artillery, but demands equality in defensive armaments. Fife will return to Berlin soon to report on the impact of Hitler's proposals in London. According to Berlin sources, Berliners criticize France for being stubborn, severe, and slow in its progress. They believe that direct negotiations are the best way to reach a lasting solution. They welcome holding a four-power conference after the main principles have been agreed upon through separate negotiations. (16th Reuters Dispatch)

Overview of Soviet Russian Armaments: Current Total Military Strength Reaches 1.3 Million; Adopting a "National Defense First" Doctrine; Carrying Out Thorough Militarization 54

World Press Moscow News: The Soviet government sings high-sounding slogans such as complete or partial disarmament to the outside world, propagates anti-war ideology, and appears to be the embodiment of peace. However, internally, it is calmly and thoroughly carrying out its most thorough militarization, adopting a "national defense first" doctrine and giving priority to undertakings related to national defense compared to other undertakings. Especially in the Five-Year Plan, it exerts its focus on centralization, sacrificing all other undertakings without hesitation and prioritizing compulsory armament, causing the living conditions of the people to fall to the extreme of misery. The essence of the Five-Year Plan lies in the inevitable success of military-related industries. The iron, fuel, machinery manufacturing, chemical, especially automobile, and aviation industries have increased dramatically compared to other sectors. This fact aims at increasing military capabilities, which goes without saying.

Looking at its armaments, their content and substance have been greatly enriched and improved. Especially in 1932, it increased by four infantry divisions and one cavalry division, bringing the number of infantry divisions to 76, cavalry divisions to 13, and independent cavalry brigades to 8, with a total military strength of more than 1.3 million, surpassing the imperial Russian army before the European War. Other aspects such as firepower equipment, mechanization, and chemical warfare preparations are also showing rapid progress. Survey of the Atlantic Route Completed: The Lindberghs Return Home; Flying Across Two Hemispheres, Traversing Three Continents; Covering a Distance of 28,000 Miles 57

Miami, Florida, USA. The famous American aviator Colonel Lindbergh and his wife arrived here from Maris City, Dominican Republic, Central America, at 1:05 PM today. The long-distance aeronautical science experiment flight has now concluded. The Lindberghs flew across two hemispheres, passed through three continents, and covered a distance of 28,000 miles. The flight began on July 9 of this year. The accuracy of the flight is admirable and is a great feat of aeronautical experimentation. Since this event, we hope that flights between continents will become more frequent in the near future. Although the Lindberghs did not want people to announce their arrival time and tried to avoid various formal welcomes, the crowds welcoming them upon their arrival were still very enthusiastic. However, they strongly declined the requests of reporters and photographers. After disembarking, they went through customs and immigration procedures and left by car. Their destination is unknown. (16th Havas Dispatch)

American Troops in Latin America to be Withdrawn Completely by Next June 58

(Washington) It has been learned today that the American troops stationed in Latin American countries will be completely withdrawn by next June. All Marine Corps stationed in Haiti are currently being withdrawn in succession and will be withdrawn completely within six months, leaving no one behind. According to this, the Marine Corps was sent to be stationed in accordance with the 1916 treaty to assist the country in establishing a responsible and orderly government. Later, there were several serious conflicts, the most serious of which was in 1929. Five Haitians were killed by the US Marine Corps. Therefore, US President Hoover appointed a delegation to investigate and study whether US troops should be withdrawn. The delegation then suggested a gradual withdrawal, to be completed by 1936. When President Roosevelt succeeded him, he decided to withdraw them as soon as possible. Therefore, the Navy Department and the State Department hope that they can be completely withdrawn by next June. (16th National Telegram)

Japanese and Puppet Destruction of the Chinese Eastern Railway Administration: Russia Issues a Serious Warning to the Puppet Regime; Unauthorized Replacement of Railway Personnel and Usurpation of Rights Clearly Violate the Fengtian-Soviet Agreement; Liability for Compensation for All Losses Incurred 62

(Moscow) Today, the Soviet Russian government, through its Consul-General in Harbin, issued a serious and important warning to the Manchurian puppet authorities regarding their continued implementation of anti-Russian policies in the administration of the Chinese Eastern Railway. The memorandum delivered pointed out that the puppet government was deliberately implementing a policy aimed at reducing the importance of the Chinese Eastern Railway and eliminating Soviet Russian rights over the railway's property, with the ultimate goal of completely seizing the railway. It stated that such circumstances violated the Fengtian and Beijing Agreements and made it difficult for Soviet Russia to recognize the legitimacy of the puppet officials' railway management plan. It also declared that the puppet government would bear strict responsibility for all damages suffered by the railway. Japanese Side Lacks Sincerity in Returning Yuguan; Uses Bandits and Traitors to Secretly Refuse Reception; Tao Shangming Goes to Yuguan Again to Negotiate with the Japanese; Taking Over Various Passes of the Great Wall is Even More Out of the Question; Jin Mines in Northern Hebei Are Being Exploited by the Puppet State 85

Tianjin Correspondence: Taking over the various passes of the Great Wall has been rumored for a long time, but it has not yet been implemented. This is probably due to the vast disparity in strength, making it difficult to rely on others' whims. Li Zeyi went to Changchun once to negotiate with the commander of the Japanese Kwantung Army, Hishikari, but there was not much progress. According to the Tanggu Agreement, we are taking over the various passes of the Great Wall, and the Japanese side originally had no reason to refuse. However, from the surface, the Japanese side has not refused, but in practice, it uses traitors, bandits, and puppet organizations to make us afraid of hurting the mouse and unable to take over. We cannot recognize puppet organizations as objects, so we have to negotiate with the Japanese side. The Japanese side's expression is extremely generous: whenever China takes over, the Japanese army will return the territory. As for the puppet organization, they dismiss it as another incident and are inconvenient to ask about. Tao Shangming once said that there is no problem in principle with taking over Shanhaiguan, only the takeover procedures have not yet been resolved. Although a forced takeover is made at this time, the small details can be slowly resolved. The Beiping Political Committee is the highest administrative body in North China, and its proposal is naturally more powerful than that of the provincial government. However, from the perspective of the general public, it is also believed that taking over the various passes of the Great Wall is not to be tolerated or delayed. Because the phenomenon in the counties of eastern Luoyang is like an enclave, the small number of security teams with short guns and rifles cannot cope with the large gangs of bandits with organization and background. Last time, Qi Wenping, Zhang Kuiyuan, and others ran rampant in eastern Luoyang. After several negotiations, teams were dispatched to encircle and suppress them, recovering Funing. But how long has it been before border alarms have been reported again? (On the Great Wall border near Yiyuan Pass and Taolin Pass, three to four thousand bandits, some say five to six thousand, have gathered again.) They are eager to move with bows and arrows. The supplies of grain and ammunition they need are all transported from outside the customs in heavy trucks. It is undoubtedly certain that they have a background. Zhang Xueliang has decided to return to China next month. The Japanese side (Kwantung Army) opposes Zhang's re-seizing of military power, and its intention is to make the overall situation in North China fall into long-term chaos, so as to gain profit. If Zhang still leads the old Northeast Army, then the thousands of bandits on the border wall will surely rise up, so that the thirty counties in the war zone will be plunged back into chaos. On the other hand, if Zhang does not re-seize military power, the Japanese side will never feed these thousands of bandits for a long time. When the time comes, we will still need to send personnel to negotiate and obtain understanding, and then send a security team to encircle and suppress them again, killing a group of ignorant and unconscious compatriots. Therefore, in other words, if the various passes of the Great Wall can be taken over early and equipped with appropriate security teams, the bandits will have no base for gathering and activities. Tao Shangming went to Beiping yesterday (14th) to visit the two chairmen, Huang and He, and requested instructions. He will go to Yuguan with Linyu County Magistrate Yuan Tai within days to negotiate the takeover procedures with Yiwo, the chief of the special affairs agency of the Japanese Kwantung Army. But what day the takeover will be implemented is still uncertain at the moment. However, Shanhaiguan is only one of the passes of the Great Wall line. Taking over is so difficult. Taking over the other seventy-odd passes, large and small, such as Taolin Pass, Yiyuan Pass, Lengkou Pass, Xifengkou Pass, and Gubeikou Pass, is not yet being talked about. If they are all as difficult as Yuguan, taking over one pass will require several months of negotiation. I don't know when it will be possible to take over completely. Some people say that the Japanese side has refused to return the various passes of the Great Wall based on the sentence in the Tanggu Agreement "the Japanese army returns to the Great Wall line." If this statement is true, then whether or not Yuguan is taken over is irrelevant. Even if its claim is not true, and we can completely take over the various passes of the Great Wall, the territory of Hebei Province is already incomplete. Dushan County will never be recovered, and two-thirds of Xinglong County, outside the Great Wall, cannot be recovered either. Xinglong County is the richest in gold mines. The locals are all poor farmers, watching the gold but unable to mine it. Over the years, at the end of the farming season, a group of people wearing clothes and carrying baskets went to Dashui (Xiaoshui) Daoliushui (mountain streams) places to pan for placer gold. However, the gains were limited, and each person earned no more than five or six jiao per day. It was not until last year that merchants raised funds to mine and applied to the Department of Industry for a mining license. The department sent technicians to survey the site and was surprised by the richness of the gold mine. The matter was heard by people from the Northeast, so Gao Jiyi, Zhang Xueming, and others organized a large-scale Jibei Gold Mine Company, including Ji County, Zunhua, Xinglong, and Miyun counties. They wanted to implement a trust policy. Merchants and people, because of the great profits involved, vowed to resist to the death, and they were at odds with each other. Until the war at Xifengkou and Lengkou occurred, the Jibei Company was suspended invisibly. Recently, the puppet state raised funds to prepare for mining. The Jibei Company, seeing this with envy, is also actively preparing to carry out small-scale mining in Xisi Daozi, but the gold ore here is far inferior to that in Daoliushui. (December 15th)

(2) The army and local militias should strive to cooperate, clear out remaining bandits, cut off their communication, and implement a "clear fields" strategy. (3) Vigorously implement the joint militia rural cleansing, awaken the public’s self-defense, and construct fortified towers and fortresses. (4) Appoint fair and just gentry to maintain local security, and strictly dismiss unscrupulous gentry and local tyrants. (5) Reorganize the baojia (paochia) system, investigate households, and assess township and town leaders. (6) Recruit refugees and appease the displaced. (7) Strictly seal off bandit areas. (8) Strictly prohibit selling weapons to aid bandits. (9) Prevent recruiting bandits into the army. Liu Xiang himself is currently in the rear,统筹 (tǒngchóu, making overall plans) for the army's pay and provisions, replenishing weapons and ammunition, and planning for resettlement funds in the recovered bandit areas. However, the people of Sichuan Province are poor and resources are exhausted, and it is indeed not easy to scrape together funds. (16th)

Zhang Dengsong, major general counselor, has been appointed as the chairman of the third inspection group, with staff officer Xie Erkang, adjutant Liu Jingyi, and quartermaster Hu Chunbing as members. After receiving the order, the division prepared rosters of personnel, horses, weapons, and equipment. Besides ordering the two brigades stationed in Chenliu and Weishi to come to Kaifeng for inspection, the division also appointed Chief of Staff Liu Wanben, quartermasters Ma Bei, adjutant Li Guangzhai, and ordnance officer Ma Yunhai as assisting inspectors for the first group; Ordnance Director Tong Yongguang, staff officer Ji Hao, quartermaster Dai Yongtang, and adjutant Song Yushu as assisting inspectors for the second group; and Quartermaster Director Hou Huachang, staff officer Mo Wenyu, adjutant Wang Junchuan, and ordnance officer Chuan Sixiang as assisting inspectors for the third group, in order to jointly conduct the inspection. (15th, chatter)

Xiaqing River in Shandong Province; Wuliu Sluice Project Completed; Opening Ceremony Held on the 15th 89

Jinan Dispatch: Han Fuju, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, believes that the Xiaqing River, originating in Jinan, passing through Yangjiao Canal, and reaching the sea in the east, traverses the northeastern part of the province. If steamships can pass through, it will not only facilitate transportation and increase tax revenue, but also divert water for irrigation, benefiting the people. The project is of great importance. However, due to years of disrepair, the river has become silted up. Therefore, he consulted with Zhang Honglie, Director of the Construction Department, and decided to allocate significant funds to reorganize the Xiaqing River. The Construction Department then organized the Xiaqing River Engineering Committee to specifically handle this matter. The committee was established in April of the 20th year. It simultaneously conducted surveys and designs and invited businesses to carry out construction. Up to now, the construction of the Wuliu Sluice and Bianjiazhuang Dam, as well as the reorganization of the sources of the Xiaqing River, such as Baotu Spring and Black Tiger Spring, have been completed one after another. Among them, the Wuliu Sluice project is the largest. Recently, Xu Xinwu, a member and deputy chief engineer of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, visited and praised it as the only new-style sluice in China. The Construction Department, concerned that various circles may not be fully aware, cordially invited various organizations and groups to visit on the afternoon of the 15th, and held the opening ceremony at the same time. They also invited visitors to see the Bianjiazhuang Dam and the dredging vessel at Huangtai Bridge. The Construction Department specially prepared several long-distance buses to transport the guests. The reporter was invited to attend, and the various situations are recorded below.

Chairman’s Report 90

The venue for the ceremony was set up on the north bank of the Wuliu Sluice. A mat shed was erected, with a horizontal banner hanging above, reading "Wuliu Sluice Opening Ceremony." A registration desk was set up in front of the shed. The meeting began at 2 PM. Chairman Zhang Honglie performed the rituals and reported on the purpose of the meeting, stating that the Xiaqing River Engineering Committee was established in April of the 20th year, and immediately conducted surveys and designs and invited businesses to carry out construction. Now, more than two years have passed. The completed projects include the reorganization of a part of Shequan and the construction of the sluice gates of the Wuliu Sluice and Bianjiazhuang Dam. The purpose of holding the opening of these two places is not to boast, but to allow the public to truly understand the importance of developing water conservancy. If everyone can work together and unite with one heart, continuing to repair other projects along the river will be easy. When the entire project is completed, the 40 million compatriots of Shandong Province will benefit from it. This is what the members of this committee are looking forward to. After Zhang's report, he, along with all the guests, went to the sluice gate to perform the opening ceremony. Zhang Yue, Zhang Honglie, Zhou Xiuwen, and Cao Liqing rotated the opening and closing mechanisms on both banks. First, the water volume was gradually released, and the gate slowly opened in a figure-eight pattern. The ships moored outside the gate passed through one after another. After the ships passed, the gate was closed again. Compared with the old sluice gates, ship navigation is much more convenient and without danger.

Sluice Gate Opening Conditions 91

(1) The Wuliu Sluice is located about nine li north of Jinan City, east of the old Wuliu Sluice. It is a double-gate type, with a gate opening of 92 meters wide, a sluice chamber of 100 meters long, a bottom width of 12 meters, and bank slopes of 1.5 to 1. The sluice pier is made of granite blocks. One row of sheet piles is driven upstream and downstream of each of the two gates and sluice piers to increase the seepage path. The sheet piles are 7.5 centimeters thick and 5 meters long. An arched stone洞 (dòng, cave/hole) is built inside the pier, 1.2 meters wide, 1.35 meters high in the center, and 75 centimeters high on both sides, for filling and draining water in the sluice chamber. The洞 (dòng, cave/hole) is equipped with an iron sliding door for opening and closing. Wooden闸 (zhá, sluice gate) doors are installed on both the upper and lower sluice gates, each door being 6 meters wide. The upper gate is 3.85 meters high, and the lower gate is 7.15 meters high. Each gate is equipped with an iron butterfly-style water gate, two holes that open and close simultaneously with the墩内 (dūn nèi, inside the pier) 洞 (dòng, cave/hole) to increase the drainage volume and save navigation time. The涵問 (hán wèn, culvert) sliding doors and butterfly-style water gates are all equipped with iron mechanisms for opening and closing. (2) After the Wuliu Sluice opening ceremony was completed, the attendees went to visit the Bianjiazhuang Sluice Gate. The construction of this gate had been completed long ago. The terrain is upstream of the Wuliu Sluice, and its structure is similar to the Wuliu Sluice, but smaller. There is also a spillway and a movable dam south of the gate. When the amount of water is regulated by the mountain洞 (dòng, cave/hole), there are more than a dozen 对槽 (duì cáo, facing each other) boats in the sluice, waiting for the sluice to open and pass. After the sluice is opened, ships接 (jiē, connect) each other順流 (shùnliú, downstream) without much effort. Outside the lower sluice gate, there is the "Jinan" dredging vessel, self-made by the Shandong Construction Department’s Hydraulic Machinery Manufacturing Plant, dredging mud. Observers on both banks are congested, and the scene is very lively.

Engineering Expenses 92

The Wuliu Sluice project cost a total of 216,814.63 yuan. The Bianjiazhuang Sluice project cost a total of 122,755.27 yuan. The A-section of the Shanshui Canal project cost a total of 33,073.51 yuan. The B-section of the Shanshui Canal project cost a total of 91,728.46 yuan. The Baotu Spring project cost a total of 3,605.17 yuan. The Black Tiger Spring project cost a total of 1,337 yuan. The Jinan dredging vessel cost a total of 19,870 yuan. The Jinan dredging project cost a total of 12,209.2 yuan. The Jinan additional mud unloading vessels cost a total of 1,020.5 yuan. The Huangtai and Shicun dredging vessels cost a total of 146,000 yuan. The total expenses above amount to 648,413.24 yuan. (16th)

Seven Officers and Soldiers of the Pixian Police Force Sentenced to Death; Joined the Communist Party and Conspired to Riot 93

Xuzhou Dispatch: The Pixian Police Brigade, instigated by reactionary elements, joined the Communist Party and conspired to riot. After receiving a report, the Central Government secretly ordered She Nianci, the Administrative Commissioner of the 12th District of Jiangsu Province, to handle the matter. On October 6th of this year, She, under the pretext of convening a joint inspection of the Tongshan, Pixian, and Suining county police forces, gathered the Pixian police force at Xiaotashan, east of Xuzhou. That night, he secretly ordered the Tongshan and Suining county police forces and the 12th District Security Regiment to surround and disarm the Pixian police force, confiscating more than 200 guns. Thirty-nine key officers and soldiers were arrested on the spot and taken to Xuzhou for interrogation. After repeated investigations, it was found that seven individuals, including Zhou Zhankui, Li Qichang, Wang Shengtang, Niu Qingchen, Wang Deyin, Gong Ziyi, and Zhang Zhendong, were deeply involved. The transcripts were compiled and reported to the Central Government for judgment and then submitted to the Provincial Government for approval. They were executed by firing squad this morning (16th). The remaining officers and soldiers were punished or released separately. Thus, the plot of the Pixian police force to riot, which had been brewing but not yet erupted, came to an end. The proclamation is recorded below: "Case investigation revealed that officers and soldiers of the Pixian Police Brigade joined the Communist Party. The undersigned (the Administrative Commissioner) previously arrested 39 officers and soldiers, including Zhou Zhankui, by name. After consultation with the Central Government’s Special Commissioner, we conducted separate interrogations and the Special Commissioner drafted handling measures. The transcripts were submitted to the Central Government for review. The Central Government then issued separate judgments, forwarding them to this office. Furthermore, the case was submitted to the Provincial Government for review, and the Jiangsu Provincial Government issued instruction 民字 (Mín Zì) No. 1603, stating that all submitted documents had been submitted to the Provincial Government meeting for discussion. It was resolved to handle the matter according to the handling measures decided by the Central Government’s Special Commissioner, and the record was filed. The seven 共匪 (gòngfěi, communist bandits) Zhou Zhankui, Li Qichang, Wang Shengtang, Niu Qingchen, Wang Deyin, Gong Ziyi, and Zhang Zhendong were all sentenced to death. It is appropriate to record the case and order the commissioner to comply with the order. This order is hereby issued for general notification." Following this, the seven 共匪 (gòngfěi, communist bandits) Zhou Zhankui and others were identified, escorted to the execution ground, and executed by firing squad. A report was also submitted. This proclamation is urgently issued for general knowledge.

Overall Salt Affairs Situation in China; Annual Salt Production Reaches 37 Million Dan; Monthly Tax Revenue Increases by 3 Million Yuan 94

Beijing Dispatch: Since the Northeast customs duties were seized by the Japanese puppets, the annual loss of national tax revenue has reached 40 million yuan, and the burden of various debts guaranteed by customs duties has thus increased sharply. In terms of salt affairs, since the Japanese forcibly occupied the salt inspection agencies in the three northeastern provinces in March of the 21st year, all salt tax revenue in the three provinces, including foreign debt installments, has been intercepted, resulting in a loss of 33 million yuan. Since the former Finance Minister Song Ziwen carefully reorganized the salt affairs, merging the salt transport offices with the inspection bureaus, eliminating corruption, and increasing the salt tax revenue. In the past, the monthly revenue was 2 million, but now it has increased to 5 million. This newspaper has inquired about the overall situation of the national salt affairs after the reorganization from the Ministry of Finance and the Salt Affairs Administration, and the details are recorded as follows.

Loss of Salt Tax Seized in the Northeast 95

In the 21st year of the Republic, the total national revenue from salt tax reached 155,212,000 yuan. Since the "September 18th Incident" occurred, 363,700 square miles of land and a population of 30 million have been lost, resulting in a reduction of 3.6 million dan of salt sales nationwide, and a direct loss of 33 million yuan in tax revenue. The stagnation of national finance and the impact on the operation of the salt industry are even greater. Therefore, the indirect losses are countless.

New Plan for Reorganizing Salt Affairs 96

In addition to the plans previously drafted by Song Ziwen that have been implemented one after another, Kong Xiangxi has recently redrafted a new, comprehensive plan to reorganize national salt affairs. The main points are as follows: (1) The national salt affairs are currently divided into 11 administrative regions, which are jointly managed by inspection agencies. The merger of these agencies can increase efficiency, save expenses, eliminate bad practices, reduce costs, and expand sales channels. (2) The整理 (zhěnglǐ, reorganize) of tax rates: The tax rates in various regions are inconsistent, which easily leads to dumping and facilitates smuggling. After the 整理 (zhěnglǐ, reorganize), the disparity in tax rates is no longer as high as before. In the future, they will gradually be unified, making it easier to collect taxes on the spot. (3) The gradual abolition of the anti-smuggling and administrative agencies at the sales outlets will increase tax revenue and reduce expenditures. This is the main point of the plan to 整理 (zhěnglǐ, reorganize) salt affairs.

Salt Tax Increases by 3 Million Per Month 97

In the past, the surplus salt tax was remitted to the Ministry of Finance by the Salt Affairs Inspection Bureau. Usually, it was only more than one million per month, and at most two million. Since Song Ziwen reorganized the salt affairs and merged the salt transport offices with the Salt Affairs Inspection Bureau, the salt administration procedures have become more convenient, and the salt tax revenue has greatly increased. Currently, 5 million yuan is remitted to the Ministry of Finance every month, and a preparatory fee has been collected since mid-September, at the rate of one 角 (jiǎo, 1/10 of a yuan) per salt transport ticket, specifically for the construction of salt warehouses and to subsidize poor sailors in the 12 Weirs. About 100,000 yuan can be collected per month. After the new plan is implemented in the future, revenue will definitely increase further.

Statistics on the Quantity of Salt Produced Nationwide 98

According to salt officials, the quantity of salt produced nationwide is the most significant in Changlu, Southern Sichuan, Shandong, and Northern Huai. The following quantities of salt were produced nationwide last year (unit: dan): (1) Changlu: 4,439,000; (2) Southern Sichuan: 4,443,000; (3) Northern Huai: 7,565,000; (4) Shandong: 7,569,000; (5) Hedong: 891,000; (6) Northern Kou: 207,000; (7) Northern Jin: 194,000; (8) Yangzhou: 609,000; (9) Songjiang: 188,000; (10) Liangzhe: 4,222,000; (11) Fujian: 1,002,000; (12) Guangdong: 3,967,000; (13) Yunnan: 488,000; (14) Northern Sichuan: 1,447,000; (15) Gansu, Ningxia, and Xinjiang combined: 162,000. The total is 37,504,000 dan.

Robbery in Xiaokunshan and Hengshan, Songjiang 99

In a temple in Xiaokunshan, the ninth district of this county, there lived a vegetarian who worshiped Buddha. Unexpectedly, a pirate ship suddenly arrived the other night, and seven or eight bandits jumped out, broke down the door, and entered. They frightened the people in the temple into silence, locked them in a room, and robbed them before fleeing with loud cries. That same night, a certain surname in a tomb house in Hengshan was also robbed by the same bandits. The losses were not significant.

Suicide Due to Economic Pressure 100

Zhang Qiusheng, a flower seller and local police officer in Sijing Township, has recently been experiencing increasing household expenses and a worsening livelihood. He borrowed a title deed from the Catholic Church, the owner of the land, a few years ago to mortgage it for cash. Recently, the church demanded the return of the title deed, but Zhang could not provide it. Last night, he secretly held a kitchen knife and tried to slit his own throat. Fortunately, the blade was rusty and dull, and the trachea was not severed, so there is no immediate danger to his life. He was carried by his son to Songjiang Hospital for treatment.

Rebuilding of Jingguang Bridge in Suzhou Completed 101

Jingguang Bridge, located outside Xumen in Hengtang, was built during Emperor Gaozong’s southern inspection during the Qing Dynasty and destroyed during the Hong Yang Rebellion. This spring, Hui Hong, the head of the Mudu Autonomous Region, planned to build the Su Mu Road, considering the bridge a vital passage between the city and the countryside. He planned to rebuild it, and Zhang Jinyuan, a Suzhou native living in Shanghai, volunteered to fund the construction of the bridge. Shi Junqing, Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, Liu Daxuan, the Chief of the First District of the City, and others jointly managed the matter. The bridge was entirely built of steel and concrete and renamed Jinyuan Bridge. It has now been completed. Yesterday (17th), the completion ceremony was held. More than a thousand people, including representatives from various organizations and groups, participated. Several steamships were specially chartered to transport them. During the ribbon-cutting ceremony, following the example of the completion of the Haizhu Bridge in Guangzhou, ten elders were invited to cut the ribbon: Wang Yunzhai, Shi Songting, Deng Jinshan, Qian Rongshan, Cao Runqing, Yan Chunsheng, Xie Baisheng, Zhu Wuting, Wang Nianci, and Zhang Yilin. Among them, Wang Yunzhai was the oldest at ninety-two years old, and Zhang Yilin was the youngest at sixty-seven years old. Therefore, Zhang specifically changed his name to "Zhang Xiaodi" when signing. Wang Yunzhai and Shi Songting gave speeches, stating that they had passed through the former Jingguang Bridge countless times when traveling between the city and the countryside before it was destroyed.

Wuxi to Add Four Postal Branches 102

Since Wu Shuqi became the head of the first-class post office in this county, he has been making every effort to 整頓 (zhěngdùn, reorganize) postal services. In order to develop postal services, he submitted a request to the Postal Administration to add a fourth branch near Yingyou Bridge in the West Gate. All plans and facilities have been reported for approval and will be implemented as soon as approval is granted.

Labor Disputes at Two Silk Factories Demanding Wages 103

In recent years, the silk market has plummeted, and the silk factories are in extreme recession, leading to repeated disputes. Taixin Silk Factory in Changfeng Bridge, Huangnitou, stopped work on the 24th of last month due to excessive losses. However, it owed its employees about 7,000 yuan in wages, which it could not pay. Therefore, the manager of the factory, Xu Junjie, set fire to the cocoon warehouse on the night of the shutdown, intending to use the insurance compensation to repay the employees' wages. However, the compensation has not yet arrived, so the employees' wages have been repeatedly delayed. On the morning of the day before yesterday, more than 400 employees gathered at the factory to collect their wages. Xu Junjie was unable to cope with the situation, and the employees suddenly started a commotion, taking Xu to the Silk Factory Labor Union in Nancangmen. Mediation failed, so they took Xu to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau for temporary detention. The employees then caused a disturbance at the labor union all night. Yesterday morning, they elected thirteen representatives, including Hua Yongbo, Su Amei, and Yin Hedi, and under the leadership of Qian Qixia, a member of the Labor Union Committee, they went to the County Party Headquarters and the County Government to petition. County Magistrate Yan advocated that Xu Junjie be transferred to the court for handling, so Xu was still detained in the Public Security Bureau yesterday. In addition, Qingfeng Silk Factory outside the South Gate also closed down last month, owing its employees more than 5,000 yuan in wages. After repeated demands without success, more than 300 people gathered at the factory around 4 PM yesterday, sitting down and demanding payment. The factory manager, assistant manager, chief accountant, and work director had all fled, leading to a conflict between the employees and Shen Guoheng, who was in charge of miscellaneous affairs at the factory. The large dining table and other items in the room were damaged. The chief of police Gong Baoda of the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau led the police to the scene to suppress the situation and took the employee representatives and Shen Guoheng and others to the bureau for investigation by the headquarters.

Civil Affairs Hall Inspector Comes to Changshu for Inspection 104

Zhao Shu, an inspector from the Civil Affairs Hall, came to Changshu on the 14th. At first, he was quite secretive, but the county government discovered him the next day and accompanied him to inspect various agencies. On the 16th, County Magistrate Zhou Heng and Public Security Bureau Chief Yin Peng accompanied him to inspect the district administration and coastal defense in Meili and Hupu. Zhao convened a meeting with the township and town leaders, considering their knowledge too immature and the coastal defense still solid. He returned to the city that night. On the morning of the 17th, he hosted representatives from various circles to solicit opinions. In the afternoon, he inspected Micheng Town in the 14th District. During this inspection, Inspector Zhao paid close attention to the rural economy. Furthermore, County Magistrate Zhou Heng, who had been repeatedly accused of smoking opium, was also subject to strict investigation to determine the truth. Zhao stayed in Changshu for about two days before returning to the province to report.

Zhenjiang, Jiangsu Province, Dredges the Liutang River 105

Xu Dingkang, Director of the Northern Jiangsu Canal Engineering Bureau and concurrently Director of the Liutang River Engineering Office, has actively been planning for dredging the river since he went to Qingjiangpu to set up an office, in order to complete this important construction project in Northern Jiangsu. Engineers have been assigned to each section of the project, but the specific construction methods need to be determined quickly. Therefore, he will convene a meeting of the county magistrates of the counties along the river to discuss the dredging of the Liutang River. Attendees include Lu Cangeng, the county magistrate of Huaiyin County, Liu Pingshi, the technical director; Sun Yuanjue, the technical director of Siyang County; Chen Tongshou, the county magistrate of Lianshui County, Wang Youting, the technical director; Shen Jinghua, the county magistrate of Muyang County, Xie Yantan, the technical director; Wen Qinming, the county magistrate of Donghai County, Xi Ye, the technical director; Fan Chengzhen, the technical director of Guanyun; Chief Engineer Ge Hanlou; engineers Chen Yuezhong, Feng Qie, Wu Guoxian, Yan Jinbo; advisor to the engineering office Wu Tongju; and dozens of others. The meeting, chaired by Xu Dingkang, resolved the following key points: (1) The establishment date of the engineering offices for each section: Huaiyin, Lianshui, and Siyang counties will be established on the 18th of this month; Shuyang, Guanyun, and Donghai counties will be established on the 20th of this month. (2) Locations of engineering offices for each section: Donghai and Guanyun will be located in Wuzhuang; Shuyang will be located in Yangkou; Lianshui will be located in Shenwan; Huaiyin will be located in Caijiaji; and Siyang will be located in Shiji. (3) The section chiefs and engineers will be responsible for preparing for the commencement of work in each section immediately, no later than January 1st. (4) Since the construction period for each section coincides with the winter defense period, the office should request Chairman Chen of the Provincial Government to add troops and increase military strength to ensure security and maintain order. (5) The number of squad leaders and team leaders should be determined based on the actual situation. (6) Prominent, respected, and impartial gentry should be invited to serve as advisory committee members in each section, in a honorary capacity. (7) Each section chief should visit the construction site at least once or twice a week to facilitate the progress of the project. In addition, the engineering office is actively conducting surveying work for each section and has organized three surveying teams. The first team is surveying from Liu Lao Jian to Qianjia and from Yaoxu Factory to Yanhetou. The second team is surveying from Qianjiaji to Xinjizhou. The third team is surveying from Xinjizhou to Longgou. They departed for surveying the day before yesterday (15th). Construction will commence after the surveying is completed.

Jiangyin, Provincial Government Orders Investigation into the Shooting of a Small Customs Patrol Boat 106

At 4:30 PM on the 3rd of this month, customs officers from the Jiangyin sub-customs office were patrolling the Jiang surface in Huangshan Port on a small customs patrol boat when they saw a civilian ship heading upstream. The ship was quite small and did not appear to be carrying any cargo, so they did not order it to stop for inspection. Unexpectedly, gunshots were suddenly heard from the ship. About ten people in military uniforms were seen on board. When the customs boat was about 50 yards away from the ship, the ship opened fire on the customs boat in several volleys. Several bullets hit the steel plate of the bow of the boat. The customs officers ordered the sailors on board to curl up and take cover and to steer to a safe place. At that time, the civilian ship continued to fire frequently at the customs boat, resulting in one bullet hitting the deck board of the stern cabin and one bullet hitting the face of the cook near the water tank. The civilian ship then sailed towards the Shixu Port area. A small boat loaded with cargo was seen following behind it. However, at the time of the incident, a ship of the Weijiang Company was also passing through the area heading upstream, so it was suspected that the civilian ship was protecting the loading and unloading of smuggled goods. The customs patrol boat then sailed to Huangtiangang, where the customs officers reported the shooting incident to the nearby water police team and requested their pursuit and protection. However, the people in the team claimed that the captain was not present, the number of water police was small, and the equipment was insufficient, making it difficult to respond. Later, Zhu Wenchao, the director of the sub-customs office, reported the incident to the Superintendent of the Zhenjiang Customs and sent a letter to the provincial government. The day before yesterday, the provincial government ordered the county government and the water police team leader to instruct the responsible personnel to conduct a thorough investigation and report the shooting civilian ship. Yesterday (14th), County Magistrate Ruan ordered the Public Security Bureau to investigate.

The Bandit Leader Chen Yuke Captured in Nantong 107

According to a secret report received by District Chief Gong of the Fifth District of the Zhenjiang Provincial Water Police, the notorious sea bandit leader Chen Yuke was gathering followers in Nantong. Inspector Qin Kunshan was dispatched to Nantong to investigate and apprehend him. On the night of the 15th, at 12:00 AM, Chen the bandit was captured at room number 12 of the Tao Zhi Hua Hotel. Two pistols and over fifty rounds of ammunition were found on his mistress, Xie Su. Both were escorted to Zhenjiang on the 17th.

Summary of the Jiaxing County Government Meeting 108

The Jiaxing County Government held a county government meeting on the previous two days, and the following important cases were resolved: (1) The current County Administrative Meeting was held on the 15th, designating Chen Youkai and Hu Daying as recorders, and each bureau and section allocated one clerk. (2) The Jiaxing Chamber of Commerce previously requested the Hebao case team to install electric lights, resulting in a loss of 267.12 yuan of silver. It was requested to be reimbursed from the county tax reserve fund. Resolution: The county tax reserve fund has been used for advances and no savings remain. This loss of lighting installation fees for the Hebao troops should be submitted to the Security Office for reimbursement. (3) The ten surplus patrol boats received by the county government under orders were handed over to the County Public Security Bureau to hire craftsmen to repair and convert into six boats, which were issued to the 2nd, 3rd, 4th, 5th, 6th, and 7th Public Security Bureaus for use as water patrols. The repair costs were paid from the accumulated police funds.

Landlords in Jiaxing report that the collection of grain taxes is very strict, but the authorities do not care about the landlords' collection of rent, which is unfair. Pinghu County Magistrate Issues Arrest Warrant for the Main Culprit in a Gambling Case 110

In the inner room of Wang Gongchang's dyeing workshop on East Main Street in this city, there has been a very large gambling den for many years. A few nights ago, someone reported it to the County Public Security Bureau, which ordered the police to arrest them. Forty-four people were captured on the spot, and over seventy or eighty people scattered and fled in the chaos. After being sent to the county, the trial commissioner, Tu Zhitong, sentenced them to fines ranging from 70 to 500 yuan, totaling over 5,000 yuan. The money on the table was confiscated. After the incident, the local residents, including Ji Shangying, learned that the mastermind behind this was Zuo Chunzheng, the former secretary of the county government, and jointly telegraphed the provincial authorities to investigate. Zuo left south on the Pingza Highway bus the day after the incident. County Magistrate Zhang Zhouwen learned of this and immediately telegraphed the Zha Pu Public Security Bureau to arrest him. Unexpectedly, this telegram had just arrived, and Zuo had already taken a bus to Shanghai. It is now heard that the county government has issued an arrest warrant to capture Zuo and other criminals to bring them to justice and investigate the matter thoroughly.

Xiao Shan Man Committed Suicide After Being Robbed of Remittance Money 111

In Shanjia Dai, a village in the western suburbs of Xiao Shan, a resident named Shan Yongxing had 100 yuan of remittance money from relatives in Hangzhou stolen on the way. After crossing the river to Xinliangting, he thought he had no face to go home, so he hanged himself. Bystanders tried to rescue him, but his spirit had already departed for the afterlife.

Ningbo's Douwei Town Plundered by Bandits 112

Douwei Town in the third district of Yuyao, located about ten li from Mazhu, was suddenly attacked by more than twenty bandits at about 6:00 PM on the previous day (the 14th). Each held pistols and wooden-cased guns, and they divided into groups to guard the entrances of the streets and fired their guns to create a show of force, cutting off traffic. They broke into various shops and looted them, including: Tongshi Dyeing Shop was robbed of thirty bolts of white cloth and over one hundred yuan in cash; Wanfeng Grocery Store was robbed of over fifty yuan in cash and eight hams; Wanshun Grocery Store was robbed of over thirty yuan in cash and countless goods; Renhe Cigarette Shop was robbed of three packs of Fairy brand cigarettes, one can of kerosene, and dozens of silver coins; Shenghe Grocery Store was robbed of over seventy yuan in paper money; Mao Pengji Cloth Store was robbed of dozens of bolts of cloth and over ten yuan in paper money; Tongxing Money Shop was robbed of over thirty silver dollars; Tongxing Silk Shop was robbed of dozens of bolts of silk cloth; and Changsheng Grocery Store was robbed of over twenty yuan in paper money and over ten hams, totaling thousands of yuan.

News from Our City: Four Party Departments Again Request That the Central Government Immediately Dispatch a Large Army to Publicly Punish Fujian 113

According to the Guomin News Agency, the Shanghai Special City Party Department, the Two-Road Special Party Department, the Seamen's Special Party Department, and the Security Team Special Party Department stated that the Fujian Incident has lasted for almost a month. Chen Mingshu, Li Jishen, and others created this rebellion and are criminals against the party and the nation, and must not be tolerated any longer. Yesterday, they jointly telegraphed the central government again, requesting that the National Government immediately dispatch a large army and publicly punish them. The original telegram is transcribed as follows: Urgent, respectfully to the Nanjing Central Executive Committee: Chen Mingshu, Li Jishen, and other rebels, under the pretext of public opinion, organized the so-called People's Government in Fujian, changed the era name and system, usurped the title and enjoyed themselves, destroyed the party and betrayed the country, colluded with bandits and sided with the enemy. Any one of these crimes is unforgivable. We have previously telegraphed requesting a public punishment. However, the incident has lasted for almost a month, and we have not seen any orders issued to punish them, and we have heard that some people advocate resolving it through political means. Our associations are deeply shocked. We believe that the rebellion created by the rebels Chen and Li is a crime against the party and the nation, and must not be tolerated any longer. Otherwise, ambitious people will follow suit, and our country will never have hope of stability. We feel a sense of danger and dare not remain silent. We are telegraphing again to earnestly request the National Government to immediately dispatch a large army and publicly punish them, and to ensure that the rebels Chen and Li are brought to justice and punished to uphold the national law and discipline. We are extremely anxious in this telegram. The Shanghai Special City Executive Committee, the Two-Road Special Party Department, the Seamen's Special Party Department, and the Security Office Special Party Department, together bow.

Yang De Zhao Discusses the Loan from Guangdong Province: The Provincial Bank's Cash Reserves for Banknotes, Amounting to Approximately 60 Million, Have Been Almost Completely Used; This Loan Is Entirely for Financial Regulation 114

According to the Xinxin News Agency, Yang Dezhao, the representative in Beijing of Chen Jitang, the Commander-in-Chief of the Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army, arrived in Shanghai on the overnight express train from Beijing the night before, awaiting a ship to go south to Guangdong to report to Chen. Yesterday morning, a reporter from the Xinxin News Agency visited him at his residence on Avenue Amyot, and he discussed in detail the motives and process of Guangdong Province's request for a loan. The details are as follows:

Motivation for the Loan 115

Yang replied to the reporter's question, first stating that since the 20th, 21st, and 22nd years, the financial situation in Guangdong Province has become increasingly strained. The Provincial Bank's cash reserves for banknotes have been almost completely used, totaling 30 million yuan. The other various public bonds and other items have also been collected and used up, amounting to no less than 30 million yuan. The two together total about 60 million yuan, which is the financial deficit of the province, and must be urgently rescued. Moreover, this deficit originally belonged to the central government, and the central government should assist Guangdong Province in seeking ways to rescue it. Therefore, the motivation for Guangdong's request for this loan is to seek financial rescue.

Request Process 116

Yang continued, "The Guangdong Provincial Bank was formerly the Central Bank. After the Central Bank established its head office in Shanghai, the Central Bank in Guangdong was reorganized last year and named 'Guangdong Provincial Bank,' which is the current Provincial Bank. The accounts, etc., still follow the old rules of the former Central Bank. The banknotes issued by the former Central Bank, except for the ten-yuan notes which have not yet been exchanged, have all been exchanged for new Provincial Bank notes. However, the cash reserves in the bank are very empty, as I mentioned earlier. Because the reserves are empty, whenever problems occur, it often leads to runs, which are difficult to deal with. For example, after the outbreak of the Fujian Incident, Guangdong experienced a run due to frequent rumors. Fortunately, the authorities responded effectively and were able to overcome it safely. The process of requesting this 15 million yuan loan was that the Guangdong authorities had already contacted and agreed with the central government in advance. I attended the Central Standing Committee meeting only to explain the reasons. The method is for Guangdong Province to directly raise funds from the Hong Kong and Guangdong banking community, and request the central government to designate a guarantee. The central government generally has no problem with this. As for what exactly will be designated as a guarantee, it has not yet been decided, but it will probably be the subsidy fee allocated by the central government to Guangdong Province as a guarantee, which is also unknown."

Leaving Shanghai Within Days 117

Continuing the conversation, he said, "I plan to leave Shanghai on the President Hoover liner tomorrow (the 19th) and return south to Guangdong. This trip has no mission, it is entirely for private affairs, in addition to celebrating my father's 70th birthday, and also dealing with the affairs of the Bohe Middle School that I founded. The school is located in my hometown of Dabu and focuses on labor education, etc."

The French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association Sends a Letter to the French Consulate to Negotiate the Jin Xi Arrest Case and Requests a Protest to the Japanese Consulate 120

The French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association, regarding the illegal arrest of naturalized Chinese citizen Jin Xi by the Japanese Consulate, sent a letter to the French Consulate General in Shanghai yesterday to negotiate, requesting that a serious protest be made to the Japanese Consulate as soon as possible to protect our national sovereignty. The original letter is recorded as follows: "Respectfully, regarding the case of the Japanese Consulate General in Shanghai illegally arresting Jin Xi, who has been naturalized as a Chinese citizen, in the French Concession, we have verified that Jin Xi's father, Jin Yongduo, was naturalized in China on October 15th of the 18th year of the Republic of China, obtained Nationality Permit Certificate No. 67 from the Chinese Ministry of the Interior, and clearly stated the age of his eldest son Jin Xi. The First Batch of American Wheat Will Be Imported This Afternoon: Berthing at Buoys No. 4 and No. 5, Unloading Will Begin Tomorrow Morning; Tax-Exempt Import of Goods Has Been Undertaken by Chinese Merchants 121

Regarding the purchase of American cotton and wheat by our government, the transportation matters are undertaken by the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. The first batch of American wheat did not arrive yesterday, and is now scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at 2:00 PM this afternoon, berthing in the Huangpu River. Unloading will begin tomorrow. The details are as follows:

Strict Secrecy 122

The state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company chartered a vessel from the American-owned Flett & Co. to transport American-loaned cotton and wheat to China. The first batch of American wheat, 8,940 tons, was loaded on the SS Aliebra Bank on the 20th of last month and set sail from North America to Shanghai via the Pacific Ocean and Japan. The shipowner previously telegraphed that it was scheduled to enter the Wusongkou at 4:00 PM yesterday and berth at buoys No. 16 to No. 17 on the Huangpu River off Yangshupu Lan Road. However, the Central Bank's US Cotton and Wheat Office, the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and the American-owned Flett & Co. all kept this matter strictly secret, so the vessel was not seen entering port at 5:00 PM.

Import This Afternoon 123

At 5:30 PM, an investigation was conducted at buoy No. 16 in the Huangpu River, and it was learned that the vessel had indeed not arrived in Shanghai. Then, inquiries were made to the shipping industry, and it was confirmed that the master of the SS Aliebra Bank telegraphed Shanghai at 1:00 PM yesterday, reporting that the vessel had encountered fog en route and would not be able to enter the Wusongkou until 2:00 PM today. The original plan was to berth at buoys No. 16 to No. 17, but because those buoys were already occupied by transport vessels, the Jianghai Customs notified Flett & Co. to change the berthing to buoys No. 4 to No. 5.

Tax-Exempt as Before 124

After our Ministry of Finance promulgated the collection of import duties on foreign rice, wheat, and flour starting on the 16th of this month, the first batch of American wheat was originally scheduled to be imported on the 11th of this month. Because the vessel encountered fog en route, the import would inevitably be subject to import duties today. After the Central Bank's US-Loaned Cotton and Wheat Office contacted the Ministry of Finance, it was decided to exempt it from taxes. All customs clearance procedures have been completed. However, all future imports of American-loaned cotton and wheat must be subject to import duties in accordance with regulations.

Unloading Tomorrow Morning 125

The first batch of American wheat, 8,940 tons, has been purchased by Chinese flour mills. After the vessel arrives in Shanghai today, it has been decided to start unloading tomorrow morning. First, the various Chinese flour mills will directly extract it and store it in their warehouses. The remaining American wheat will still be stored in the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Chinese warehouse or the Yangtze Wharf. The vessel, after being unloaded, will be loaded with our country's export goods to the United States.

Java Opens a Nanyang Express Ship: Can Reach Batavia in Eleven Days 127

Only the Dutch Java Company operates commercial ships on the Shanghai route to Java in the South Seas Islands. Its business has traditionally focused on the import of Java sugar and the export of Chinese soybeans. This year, the import and export business is quite sluggish. In order to attract business, the company has opened an express ship, and its plan to reach Nanyang in eleven days is urgently recorded below to inform those concerned about shipping.

Sharp Decline in Freight 128

Most of the sugar sold in our country is Java sugar, which is also the raw material for Dongyang sugar and is purchased from Java. After the sugar tax increased this year, the import tax exceeded the sugar price by more than three times, causing Java sugar to come to China to plummet. Sugar merchants have stopped ordering one after another, and the number of shipments has decreased sharply, causing Java shipping to also suffer this year. Now, each ship carries at most only one or two thousand tons, and sometimes only five or six hundred tons, which is less than 20-30% of the previous amount. Since the Northeast was occupied, the export of soybeans from our country, which was previously transshipped in Shanghai, has now been completely changed to Dalian. The shipment of goods from Shanghai has fallen to an extremely low level.

Limited Passengers 129

Most of the Chinese living in the South Seas Islands are from Fujian and Guangdong, so the company's ships must pass through Xiamen to facilitate the travel of overseas Chinese from Fujian Province. Recently, the authorities in the South Seas colonies have increased the head tax for Chinese going to the South Seas because the sugar and rubber industries there have been sluggish this year, and they have been particularly strict in restricting the entry of laborers. Without a familiar merchant acting as a guarantor, they are prohibited from landing, so the passenger business has also been greatly affected. There are no restrictions on consumers traveling to Nanyang.

Opening an Express Route 130

In order to develop the shipping industry, Mr. Yan Liwen of the Java Company's Shanghai Deda branch personally went to Nanyang to conduct inspections. Considering that in recent years the shipping industry has been opening express ships, regardless of the European and American routes, the sea journey has been shortened and time has been saved. Ships to the South Seas Islands have traditionally taken 26 days to reach Batavia from Shanghai. Now, in the autumn of competition, the company has also decided to launch a special express ship on the route from Shanghai to Batavia starting next month, reducing the days of docking at various places and increasing the speed at the same time. From Shanghai to Batavia, it is limited to only eleven days of sailing. It is planned to dispatch three of the largest ships, such as the 12,000-ton Zhibada, to sail. This route is currently being planned, which will shorten the journey to Nanyang by more than half and reduce the suffering of being confined to a ship.

Liu Xiang's Representative, Fan Chongshi, Returns to Shanghai: Discusses the Bandit Suppression Situation in Sichuan Province 131

Fan Chongshi, the Shanghai representative of Liu Xiang, the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in Sichuan, went to Sichuan in early October to visit Liu and make a report. He has now returned to Shanghai after completing his official duties. According to him, the communist bandits in northern Sichuan are gathered north of the Quhe River, along the Bashui River in Tongjiang, Nanjiang, Bazhong, Yilong, Wanyuan, Daxian, and Xuanhan, and their main bandit army is in Daxian and Xuanhan. There is a large mountain east of the bandit area, with no roads to travel. The other three sides, south, west, and north, are currently surrounded. The southwest is guarded by the Third Route Army of Li Jiayu and Luo Zezhou, and the Fourth Route Army of Yang -. The west is garrisoned by the Second Route Army of Tian Songyao, attacking the southern part of Yilong. The northwest is garrisoned by the First Route Army of Deng Xihou, blocking the communist bandits from fleeing to Shaanxi and Gansu. The south is garrisoned by the Fifth Route Army, the 21st Army, attacking the main force of the Red bandits. The 21st Army's Fan Shaozeng department has now crossed the Quhe River and is fighting hard. The Wang Lingji department is supporting on the right, and the progress is quite smooth.

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, the Fujian side is taking advantage of the chaotic situation and repeatedly spreading rumors of invading Zhejiang to the north, which has become increasingly urgent in recent days. According to a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency yesterday morning, the reason why Fujian dares to make this desperate gamble is that it has completed a solid military alliance with the communist bandits, forming a mutual support. The area between the central army and the so-called People's Revolutionary Army has been dominated by the communist army. The Fujian side is relying on this point as its rear, and only deploying the 19th Route Army to garrison various important places within 100 miles of the north and south coastlines. As for the Quanzhou, Zhangzhou, Haicheng, and Shima areas on the border between Fujian and Guangdong provinces, there are currently about 10,000 troops under Zhang Yan and Weng Zhaoyuan stationed there, while Nansheng, Zhangpu, Heping, Yunxiao, and Zhao'an are distributed by communist bandits. The recent deployment of the Guangdong army is for this reason. Therefore, it can be seen from the fact that the Fujian side has concluded a defensive alliance with the communist bandits. It is heard that more than 1,000 soldiers of the People's Government stationed in Shunchang and Changle recently mutinied, took up arms, and became bandits. They raised the red flag and established a Soviet government in the area, and there is deep concern that the 19th Route Army will be completely engulfed by communism.

Aviation Exhibition Postponed 135

The aviation exhibition initiated by the China Aviation Association plans to collect various air defense weapons and display them in Shanghai for three weeks starting on January 28 of next year, the anniversary of the Songhu Anti-Japanese War, so that people in Shanghai can have a better understanding of air defense weapons and arouse their interest in saving the country through aviation. (7) Regarding how to raise funds for the upcoming election expenses, it was resolved to create a budget list and have Chairman Du advance the funds. Seamen's Union Conducts Registration; Issues Notice to Seamen Yesterday 140

After the dissolution of the China Seamen's United General Association, the Central Government ordered Yang Hu and others to prepare for the establishment of the China Seamen's Union. After the association's preparations were completed, it is now actively preparing to establish branches in various regions. However, due to the inconsistency of all badges and certificates after the reorganization, the association convened a meeting of seamen's groups the day before yesterday to discuss registration methods in order to unify them. The association's notice to seamen, issued yesterday, is recorded as follows: "Dear seamen, you work day and night in the treacherous waves, sacrificing yourselves to seek happiness for the masses and survival for the nation. Such a great spirit is so glorious and admirable! However, capitalist imperialists use ruthless and insidious means to continuously ravage you, and the comprador class, acting as accomplices, oppress you one after another. What a painful and unjust thing! Our Prime Minister Sun Yat-sen, witnessing the general seamen suffering such heavy ravages and oppression, could not bear to see you forever trapped in deep water, leading an inhuman life, so he used his life's efforts to awaken you, teach you to unite and fight. In the past, with the leadership and command of our party, the Seamen's Union once blossomed brilliantly. However, during this period, due to the sabotage of the Communist Party, it fell into a state of disunity. Later, thanks to the Central Government's dispatch of personnel to reorganize, remove the muddy and retain the pure, it gradually embarked on the right path. Unexpectedly, the January 28th Incident occurred, and the Shanghai Seamen's Union Reorganization Committee had to stop working. By the time the war ended, a few seamen comrades organized the so-called Shanghai Seamen's Union Maintenance Committee. In May of this year, the Shanghai Seamen's Union Temporary Steering Committee was established, mutually undermining each other, viewing the union as a weapon, leaving our seamen at a loss. In September of this year, our association was produced under the leadership of the China Seamen's Union Preparatory Committee, taking over the former Shanghai Branch Reorganization Committee of the China Seamen's Industrial United General Association, the Shanghai Seamen's Branch Maintenance Committee, and the Shanghai Seamen's Union Temporary Steering Committee one by one. In other words, in the recent past, the chaotic situation of each governing its own affairs has been unified. Only our association is the only group for the seamen of Shanghai. However, our association has not been established for long, like a garden that has been barren for a long time. All the work must wait for the gardeners, the seamen, to work hard to cultivate and plant. In this way, our garden can gradually flourish, and a sound foundation can be built here. We also feel that the previous failure was due to the separation of the union and the workers. In fact, the union is an organized body of workers and should be maintained by all workers. As for the union, it should also stand in the position of the workers, fighting for the workers and sacrificing for the workers. This can make the union and the workers become one entity. Therefore, our current plan is: (1) to strengthen the organization and enrich the power of the national revolution; (2) to improve the treatment of workers and protect their lives; (3) to relieve the suffering of workers and improve their technical abilities; (4) to assist the government in developing routes and recovering navigation rights. Dear seamen, thinking about your interests and thinking about the completion of the national revolution, our association is determined to use great power to implement the above four plans. At the same time, we hope that you will also stand in the same position, keep pace with our association, and work together to promote the realization of this plan. We will use this to strengthen the connection between workers and the union, creating a real union that seeks benefits for the workers and demonstrates the power of the workers."

Buddhist Association: Memorial Service for Huang Maolin Yesterday; Promoting Buddhism Globally; Raised 6,000 Silver Dollars for Bereavement 143

The Chinese Buddhist Association, Shanghai Buddhist Association, and other groups held a memorial service for Layman Huang Maolin at Jueyuan at 2 p.m. yesterday. Those present included Yuan Ying, Huang Hanzhi, Guan Jiongzhi, Wen Lanting, Li Jingwei, Zhu Xiechen, and dozens of others. Yuan Ying, chairman, reported the purpose of the meeting, stating that Layman Huang Maolin, editor of the English Buddhist magazine, was the only contributor in the country who could promote Buddhism globally. He had translated the Sixth Patriarch Altar Sutra, the Amitabha Sutra, the Ten Wholesome Karma Path Sutra, and the first volume of the Consciousness-Only Treatise, which in recent years has influenced European people's inclination towards Mahayana Buddhism, and has had a good understanding of Chinese Buddhism. Two years ago, he made a vow to travel west to India to study Sanskrit and Pali Buddhist scriptures. Colleagues had supported his journey, hoping that he would return to China after completing his studies and make great contributions. Unexpectedly, on the 1st of this month, a telegram was received from a friend in Kuala Lumpur, shocking everyone with the news that Mr. Huang had tragically drowned at sea on the 28th of last month. The loss of such a rare talent in Buddhism is truly a misfortune for all beings in the degenerate age. Mr. Huang has a grandmother who is over eighty years old, a mother in good health, young siblings, and a widow and orphan, a family of more than ten, with no means of livelihood. His wife came to Shanghai after hearing the news, grief-stricken and unable to recover, unable to rise from her illness. All who mourn the unfinished cause of Mr. Huang and sympathize with his orphaned family, after holding a meeting, discussed ways to provide for the family's future life, planning to raise 6,000 yuan in bereavement funds to purchase public bonds or treasury bonds, and use the monthly interest to barely maintain their livelihood. Next, a Buddhist memorial ceremony was held, followed by a family member reporting on Mr. Huang's history and expressing deep gratitude to everyone for raising a large sum of money.

The branch in the city center area is currently laying cables. The details are recorded separately as follows:

Since the Pudong Cross-Border Machine Slow Demolition Telephone Bureau was established at the end of last month, it was originally scheduled to begin removing the 78 cross-border telephone machines in the Pudong area the day before yesterday. However, because the telephone company's transfer to the Chinese boundary's "02" manual station is unusually busy, if it is divided, it will still be connected from the central "02" manual station to the Chinese boundary's Nanshi General Bureau, and then through the Gaochang waterline to Pudong, which is inconvenient. Therefore, the Shanghai company, for the convenience of users to connect to Pudong telephones, plans to install a "04" manual station before Pudong telephones are assigned to the Telephone Bureau, specializing in the application of this after the concession calls Pudong (because Pudong cross-border telephones are mostly made to the concession), which is expected to be completed around February 10 and can be used on February 20. All Pudong's cross-border telephone machines will be completely transferred to the Telephone Bureau for operation by the end of February.

Chairman's Report 155

After performing the rituals, Chairman Wen Hongen reported, saying that today is the day of the training institute's restoration and establishment, and he felt very honored that people from all walks of life came to participate. Shanghai is an important commercial port in our country, and the need for police officers to have specialized knowledge is particularly necessary. Therefore, the local authorities specially set up a police training institute in Zhabei. Since its establishment, it has been many years. Later, due to the outbreak of the Shanghai War, the institute was temporarily suspended due to the war. Now, after several months of preparation, it has been restored. He hoped that everyone present would provide guidance from time to time to correct any shortcomings.

Mayor's Speech 156

Next, Mayor Wu gave a speech, saying that today is the opening day of the 16th session of the police training institute. The police themselves have a great relationship with the entire society. Therefore, modern civilized countries all have good police officers, because the concept of "country" is organized by three elements: sovereignty, people, and land. The various relationships that people have on the land all depend on the police to maintain and rescue. We know that the greatest purpose of a country is to use laws to protect people's lives and property. However, the law is a kind of regulation, and its implementation cannot be done without the police. Therefore, from the above theory, all modern police officers should undergo considerable training, because after they have considerable knowledge and skills, they will not fail the country's trust, and the various evils in society can also be eliminated by their power, so that the country becomes stronger day by day. Therefore, the responsibility of the police is very important. I hope that you will take what I said today as a reference for the future, work hard in your duties, and not fail the original intention of setting up the training institute and the people's taxes.

Difficult to Achieve Reconciliation in the Kaisheng-Kaijue Case 160

Kaisheng, the abbot of Guo'en Temple in this city, fearing that his fellow monk Kaijue (also the abbot of Chao Yin Cave) would seize his position as abbot, took advantage of Kaijue's visit to Shanghai to collect donations. Kaisheng secretly reported him to the Buddhist Association, luring Kaijue to Caohejing and detaining him in the Vagrant Self-Reliance Institute. Meanwhile, Kaisheng went to the mountain and forcibly took over the position of abbot of Chao Yin Cave, holding it for over a year. Now, Kaijue's secular brothers have learned of this and hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the Second Special District Local Court, accusing Kaisheng of unlawful imprisonment, etc. The court issued a document to the Vagrant Self-Reliance Institute, bringing Kaijue forward for questioning. The original and accused parties were separately released on bail pending investigation and further interrogation. During the re-interrogation the other day, the lawyers of both parties requested an extension of the deadline to facilitate reconciliation. This matter has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. It is now heard that a certain two lay Buddhists are making great efforts to mediate the matter. However, Kaijue is demanding an exorbitant sum of 15,000 yuan, while Kaisheng is only willing to pay several thousand yuan, making it difficult to reach an agreement. Moreover, Kaisheng, in view of Kaijue's various illegal acts on the mountain in the past, which led to his expulsion by his master, feels that if a large sum of money is given to him this time, he may again plot to seize his position as abbot of Guo'en Temple. Kaijue must therefore sign a written guarantee. Therefore, this matter is still difficult to reconcile amicably, and the court has already made some overtures. It is feared that it will be difficult to achieve the goal of withdrawing the lawsuit.
