The Case of the Anhui Self-Defense Corps Commander Colluding with Bandits: Detective Suspected of Extortion Sentenced 162

Zhang Sentenced to 30 Days of Detention, Suspended for Two Years 163

The former commander of the Suzhou Self-Defense Corps, the notorious bandit leader Quan Liting (also known as Guangyi) from Anhui, and Wei Zizhen (also known as Zizhong and Wei San), both committed numerous crimes in Anhui. The Anhui Provincial Government issued arrest warrants for them. They fled to Shanghai and resided at No. 3, Siming Village, Fuxu Road in the French Concession. Liu Junqing, the Chinese detective chief of the Old Zhabei Police Station in the Public Concession, learned of this. On the evening of the 3rd of this month, he sent his colleague Zhang Kewen from Anhui to Quan and Wei's residence to investigate the truth. Quan and others preemptively reported to the French Police Station, accusing Zhang of extortion of 300 yuan, requesting detention and investigation. The police chief approved the request and sent detectives to investigate, taking Zhang and Quan and Wei to the police station together. Later, the Old Zhabei Police Station sent detectives to take Quan and Wei to the First Special District Court for questioning and detention, awaiting notification from the Anhui Provincial Government to send personnel to Shanghai to extradite them. The French Police Station investigated Zhang Kewen and found that he was indeed suspected of extortion. He was sent to the Second Special District Court for prosecution. Zhang hired lawyer Jiang Yiping to defend him, and the British Police Station sent the two plaintiffs, Quan and Wei, to court for cross-examination. The court announced the conclusion of the trial, ordering Zhang to pay a deposit of 500 yuan and await the scheduled sentencing. Quan and others were taken back to the British Police Station by detectives for detention. These details have been previously reported. The other day, the sentencing date arrived. The defendant Zhang Kewen arrived in court to await instructions. At 2:30 PM, Judge Wu Fanglian presided over the first criminal court and sentenced Zhang Kewen to 30 days of detention for attempting to unlawfully obtain property from others through extortion, with a two-year suspension. The number of days of pre-trial detention will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of detention. During the appeal period, the defendant will remain on the original bail.

Spreading Seeds of Patriotism and Promoting Production to Save the Nation 167

Planned Itinerary of 30 Cities and 30,000 Li 168

According to a Shanghai News Agency report, the Shanghai National Crisis Propaganda Group, organized by Shen Yiqian and other students from the Shanghai Art School, received support from the central government in February of this year. They departed from Beijing and traveled along the Yangtze River, North China, and the Mongolian border for seven months. They passed through eleven provinces, traveled 20,000 li, and overcame numerous hardships before returning to Shanghai in September of this year. They immediately began preparing for a second long-distance propaganda campaign. It opened on December 1st at the Civic Education Center, lasting for seventeen days, and closed yesterday. The various aspects are detailed below:

Mongolia-Border Exhibition Closed Yesterday 169

The Shanghai National Crisis Propaganda Group's Mongolia-Border Northwest Exhibition, which opened on December 1st at the Municipal Public Education Center on Wenmiao Road in the West Gate, lasted for a total of seventeen days and closed yesterday. During the exhibition period, 300,000 people visited, including Wu Tiecheng, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Wu Yunzhu, Lin Pengxia, Wu Zhihao, and Du Chongyuan. Another Expedition to Depart at the End of the Month 170

The group's second long-distance national crisis propaganda campaign is scheduled to depart at the end of this month. The propaganda work will be divided into: (1) National Crisis Propaganda, such as holding national crisis painting exhibitions, anti-Japanese war relics, national goods exhibitions, and screening lantern slides and films, distributing books and pictorials, and using text and photographs to provide open propaganda to the local news media to spread seeds of patriotism; (2) Fact-Finding, such as the lives of various ethnic groups, industry and commerce, products, transportation, climate, etc., using text, drawings, photography, and other methods to collect, compile, and print into books for reference by various sectors; (3) Promoting National Goods, collecting local products, holding public exhibitions, and promoting the goal of saving the nation through production.

From Xi'an, they will pass through Hanzhong, Chengdu, Baxian, Xuanhua, Hankou, Changsha, Hengyang, Qujiang, and reach Guangzhou. From Guangzhou, they will pass through Cangwu, Kunming, Hong Kong, Shantou, and return to Shanghai. The itinerary includes a total of thirty cities and covers 30,000 li. Unless there are obstacles, the plan will not be changed, he said.

The German Starship Tested Its Guns at Song Yesterday 173

To Be Handed Over to Customs for Use Within the Year 174

The Jianghai Customs had previously commissioned the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance to build thirteen patrol ships for intercepting pirates. The ten larger ones were contracted to the Jiangnan Shipyard. The first of these, the German Starship, was launched in June, and the entire project is now complete. Yesterday morning at 8:00 AM, personnel from the Jiangnan Shipyard, together with representatives from the Customs, boarded the ship and sailed to the waters outside the Wusong Estuary to test its guns. Over ten shots were fired, and the results were excellent. The ship returned to Shanghai at 4:00 PM in the afternoon. The ship has a displacement of 700 tons, is 200 feet long, 30 feet wide, and 10 feet 6 inches deep, with a draft of 10 feet. It has a speed of 13 nautical miles per hour, one three-pound gun in the front and one in the rear, twelve machine guns, and two speedboats. It is scheduled to be handed over to Customs for use by the end of the year.

Xinhua Bookstore Accused of Selling Obscene Books 175

The Xinhua Bookstore at No. 160 Jiaotong Road, Shandong Road, published a book in September of this year called "A Comedy of Love and Money, Part 1." Since its publication, it has become very popular and sold widely. In less than three months, over 3,000 copies have been sold. Subsequently, Deng Hailin, a Chinese detective of the Political Department of the General Police Station, heard that the contents of the book were obscene. On the 10th of last month, he went to the Xinhua Bookstore and obtained a copy of "A Comedy of Love and Money." After taking it back to the police station and examining it, he found that the language was lewd and that the description of sexual intercourse was particularly detailed, which would induce sexual desire and harm public morals. He reported this to the police chief and specially requested the First Special District Court to summon the bookstore manager, Zhu Dabai, to the second criminal court yesterday morning. The police lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, presented the case, stating that he was prosecuting under Article 251 of the Criminal Code for disseminating or selling obscene literature and requested that the law be strictly enforced. He then presented the book as evidence. The defendant, Zhu Dabai, hired lawyer Jiang Chiping, who argued that the book "A Comedy of Love and Money" had been republished and released on the 25th of last month, and that all the obscene points had been automatically revised, and that a statement had been added to the preface. He then presented the revised book for inspection. Judge Deng Baosun examined the report and ordered the debate to begin. After the debate between the two lawyers, the court ordered that the case be adjourned until Tuesday of next week for sentencing.

Sanwei Nunnery Monk Accused of Stealing Electricity 176

Yuan Can, also known as Yuan Chang, the abbot of the Sanmei Nunnery outside the Small South Gate, felt that the nunnery's electricity bill was too high. In July of this year, he colluded with a craftsman named Zhang Ziming to remove an electric wire when the China Merchants Electric Company was modifying the electric meter, so that less current would flow, stealing more than 50 yuan of electricity each month. The company became suspicious and sent an investigation team to investigate and find out the truth. They requested the local court to detain Zhang Ziming, while Yuan Chang fled at the time, but was also detained later. He was subsequently released on bail. However, this case has now been prosecuted. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhang Peiming opened the eleventh court to hear the case. Yuan Can did not attend the hearing. Only Zhang Ziming testified that the electric meter was installed on a partition wall and may have fallen off due to vibration, and that he was not suspected of colluding to steal electricity. Witness Ding Hanchun testified that, according to his experience, this may have happened, but it was not within his duties, so he could not confirm it. According to Ling Kejun, the electric meter was installed, and he went to stamp it with a lead seal. He did not inspect the interior at the time, but said that it could not have fallen off unless it was removed by human force. The judge, noting that Yuan Can had not arrived, ordered that the bail be submitted after the case, and that the hearing be reconvened later. The defendant was remanded in custody.

Fire at Jisi Feier Road 177

At around 10:30 PM the other night, a straw shop opened by Bai Shixian across from the post office on Jisi Feier Road in West Shanghai caught fire. Thick smoke filled the air, and flames soared. Fortunately, the Caojiadu Fire Brigade rushed to the scene with several pump trucks to put out the fire. It was quickly extinguished. Only the shop's large straw bales were burned, and the walls were slightly damaged. It was fortunate that a major disaster was averted.

Shanghai News to Be Published Periodically 178

Recently, people from the news and legal professions, noting that the city's newspapers suspend publication during the Lunar New Year, resulting in a complete cutoff of all news, felt that those who care about national affairs and pay attention to social conditions were all feeling a sense of silence. Therefore, in order to communicate news from all sides, a New Year's Daily newspaper called "Shanghai News" will be published. It is scheduled to be published from New Year's Day, with one large sheet per day, and will be suspended on the 4th. In addition to publishing speeches by famous people every day, it will also include a large amount of domestic telegrams and local news from the city. The news reports will be written by specially assigned reporters, and will be concise, insightful, and accurate. The circulation is expected to be large, and the advertising rates will be very low. Currently, the number of advertisers is very enthusiastic. Although it is still in the preparation stage, it has already achieved such results, which is quite commendable. The office address has been determined as No. 4, Dongpuyi Lane, Qipu Road, telephone number 46606.

Robbers Reenact Robbery: Led by Police Detectives to the Scene 179

Xu Yongyuan, a Chinese detective of the Hongkou Police Station, previously arrested two robbers from Jiangbei, Zhu Mengyu and Qi Zhengbao, in a straw hut in the Jinjia House on Avenyi Road. A pistol and five bullets were found and taken to the police station, and they were sent to the First Special District Court for investigation. Yesterday, Judge Wu Zehan continued the trial in the third criminal court. The police lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, stated that during the investigation, it was found that the defendant Zhu Mengyu, at 10:30 PM on August 7th of last year, colluded with Xu Deqing and Shen Fulin, who are still at large, and Yang Chunfa (also known as Liang Yongquan), who had already been convicted and sentenced for carrying military firearms, to rob a certain cigarette and paper shop at No. 957 Donghan Bili Road. Shen fired the gun and killed the shop owner. Zhu and Liang Yongquan were lookouts outside the door. He and the police detectives went to the scene to reenact the locations where they stood during the robbery. Qi Zhengbao denied the charges and requested a hearing. Zhu Mengyu confessed without denying and said that Qi Zhengbao did not go. Judge Wu ordered that they remain in custody and that the investigation be verified again later.

Record of the Meeting of Representatives of the Chinese Cigarette Exchange Industry 180

The Shanghai Cigarette Exchange Industry Association, in order to comply with the order of the Shanghai Treasure Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Office to rectify and collect taxes in accordance with the regulations, and because the burden on the Chinese industry was at stake, specially invited responsible representatives from various districts of the Chinese area of this city at 2:00 PM the other day to hold a meeting to discuss relief policies. Committee members Qiu Tanglin, Chai Yasheng, Zhang Bingyuan, Wang Kuiyuan, Teng Zhixiang, and representatives from various districts, totaling more than fifty people, attended. Chen Liangyu, the chairman, announced the opening of the meeting, performed the rituals, and reported on the letter from the tax office. Next, the proposed solutions were discussed. It was generally agreed that the industry in the Chinese area has already effectively extinguished local tobacco. They are currently engaged in the exchange of cigarettes, which is a small business with meager profits. The various taxes and levies, if paid according to the old rules, are already a struggle to maintain. Since the January 28th Incident, all industries have declined, and business has not yet recovered. The industry has fallen further behind. With the recent increase in the unified cigarette tax and the failure to unify the increase in price, if the license fee is collected in accordance with the regulations, small shops with limited capital will find it difficult to bear the burden. The chairman should be asked to find a way to remedy the situation. The following methods were decided upon by the public: (1) Chen Liangyu and Shen Weiting were publicly recommended to negotiate with the tax authorities to reach a proper solution and continue to collect taxes according to the old rules, so as to avoid disputes and benefit both the tax authorities and the merchants; (2) If the tax authorities disregard the merchants' difficulties, they will only have to follow the procedures of the autumn of last year; (3) If the goal is not achieved, they would rather sacrifice together. The meeting was adjourned at 5:00 PM after the resolutions were passed by all members.

The 31st Branch of the Municipal Federation Was Re-elected Yesterday 181

The 31st branch of the Shanghai First Special District Municipal Federation held its third member congress at 2:00 PM yesterday. More than seventy people attended. Hu Fengxiang, a staff member of the Municipal Federation, provided guidance and supervised the election. The results of the ballot count were announced, with Fei Liangheng, Zheng Dongshan, Song Shixiang, and others elected as executive committee members. Subsequently, the proposed solutions were discussed. The merchants and residents in the area of the intersection of 界路克 and 能海 roads requested that the large iron gate of the train station be opened to facilitate traffic. It was decided that: (A) A letter should be sent to the railway bureau to petition for this; (B) Zheng Dongshan, Fei Liangheng, Huang Qiujiang, and Liang Chunlin should be publicly elected as representatives. The meeting was adjourned at 4:00 PM.

Inside Story of the Wing On Company Robbery: Hu Songshan's Deep Resentment After Being Dismissed by Wing On 184

Planned and Organized the Robbery with Accomplices Meticulously 185

The "Big Brother" Escaped Far Away with the Money: None of the Accomplices Escaped the Net 186

The Wing On Company on Nanjing Road was suddenly stormed by a gang of robbers at dusk on the 6th of this month. On the third and fourth floors, they pulled out pistols, preventing the company's delivery staff from raising the alarm. They robbed the money bag containing 18,000 yuan that the staff was carrying and fled. One of the robbers, Yan Amao, was caught on the spot, and a pistol was found on him. Subsequently, Huang Yingjie and Lang Chengpei, detectives from the Old Zhabei Police Station, together with Chief Detective You Agen, arrested three more accomplices, Feng Zuowen, Hu Songshan, and Feng's mistress, Pan Meimei. They were all sent to the First Special District Local Court and ordered to be detained pending investigation and trial. These details have been previously reported. It is now learned that the mastermind behind this case was actually Hu Songshan. Hu is from Guangdong. He used to work at the Wing On Company, but was later dismissed and became unemployed. Therefore, he had a deep

Deep Resentment 187

Although he had recently been employed in the foreign goods department of the New World Company, his old hatred had not been quelled, and he was always thinking of revenge. Half a year ago, he decided to gather a crowd to commit robbery. Because most of the staff members of Wing On were from Guangdong, the accomplices should also be from Guangdong to make it easier to carry out the plan. He invited Feng Zuowen to cooperate. After Feng secretly plotted several times, he realized that two people were too few. Feng then invited two other people and swore an oath over wine, vowing not to change their minds halfway. However, after the oath, the two disappeared without a trace. Hu and Feng knew that those people were not reliable and planned to find new comrades. Feng's mistress, Pan Meimei, introduced Yan Amao and a "Big Brother" to them. They rented Room 439 of the Dongya Hotel and met with Feng and Hu to

Agreed Harmoniously 188

On the 5th of this month, the "Big Brother" handed over two pistols and decided that the next evening, when the company's cashiers were sending the cash collected from various departments to the general accounting office, they would intercept it halfway. However, Hu felt that the "Big Brother" was not one of them and must have different intentions. He was deeply worried that after the robbery, he would swallow the proceeds alone. Therefore, he secretly instructed Feng to monitor him in secret. Unfortunately, Hu had foresight, but Feng did not take precautions. When they were about to commit the robbery, the "Big Brother" made an excuse to lure Feng away. He and Yan Amao, each carrying firearms, mixed into the company. After obtaining the huge sum of money, he fled first, leaving Yan to be captured on the spot, while he

Escaping with Funds 189

Still without a trace, only that Feng at the time did not suspect that Da Age would "forget the well after drinking the water" (abandon a tool after it has served its purpose), so he went to the New New Hotel and opened room 418 to sit and wait with Hu. However, after waiting for a long time without seeing his accomplices return, he went with his mistress, Sister Pan, to Da Age's home at 82 Rue Wagner in the French Concession to visit. Unexpectedly, at this time, Chief Detective You and others, based on Yan Amao's confession, were searching the house. Because Da Age had not returned home, they remained stationed there. When Feng and his wife arrived and were questioned and found to be accomplices, they were immediately arrested. They then went to the New New Hotel and apprehended Hu Songshan. They further searched Hu's office at the New New Company, and seized from a drawer

Numerous Letters 190

The letters included some in which bandits invited Hu to rob the Wing On Company, others in which Hu was threatened for refusing, and still others in which Hu, under his own name, reported to the Wing On Company, containing elements of self-confession. According to Hu's confession, the letters were all written by him in advance to serve as evidence after the robbery was discovered, proving that the robbery was not his intention, thereby mitigating his guilt. The meticulousness of his scheme truly left no detail unattended, and his premeditation showed that he had been planning this for a long time. Yesterday, the police escorted the bandits to the First Special District Local Court for interrogation. Police lawyer Zhang Shizhu explained the circumstances of the defendants' robbery plan and requested severe punishment. Judge Feng interrogated each bandit separately and then ordered them to be remanded in custody for continued interrogation at a later date.

Shanghai Municipal Police Department - Attention to Pudong Fire Prevention - New Fire Engine Purchased - New Association Building to be Constructed Soon 191

The Yangjing district of Pudong has recently seen increasing commercial activity and a surge in population. However, modern fire-fighting equipment is still lacking, and the traditional wooden water dragons are no longer suitable. As a result, a major fire broke out in the town this summer, causing a huge disaster with losses exceeding 100,000 yuan. Wen Hongen, the head of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, considered fire-fighting equipment extremely important and closely related to local security, so he appointed Hong Qi, the head of the bureau's Second Section, and instructed Dong Zhihe, the director of the fire-fighting division, to urge the Yangjing Town Fire Brigade to actively reorganize and re-elect Chen Quan, a man of outstanding reputation and familiar with fire-fighting conditions, as a standing committee member responsible for all internal and external affairs of the association. It is reported that the association has already purchased a new-style "Talice" (transliteration) pump fire engine and 4,000 feet of hose. When the new engine was demonstrated the other day, the entire town, young and old, went to watch, creating a lively scene with unanimous praise. As for the association building, plans have been made, requiring over 10,000 yuan, and construction will begin soon.

Zhabei Derun Road - Large Fire on Wasteland - Estimated 54 Straw Huts Burned Down - Rumor is that an Overturned Kerosene Lamp Caused the Disaster 192

In the area surrounding Liangyi Lane on Derun Road, within the jurisdiction of the Third Precinct of the Fifth District of Zhabei, because it was originally wasteland, no fewer than sixty households of poor people had built houses to live in. Feng Zhaonian, a 31-year-old man from Yancheng who buys and sells old goods, lived in straw hut number 56. Unexpectedly, at about 12:20 AM yesterday morning, a fire suddenly broke out at Feng Zhaonian's house, immediately spreading to neighboring houses. The neighbors were awakened from their dreams, fleeing in panic, shouting loudly, creating chaos and disorder. At that time, the nearby Weiyang New Stage had not yet ended its performance. Upon hearing the fire alarm, the audience scrambled to escape from the theater, with countless people being pushed to the ground, and cries of distress also rising. When the Third Precinct of the Fifth District received the report, they quickly dispatched patrol officers to the scene to maintain order, which gradually stabilized. At the same time, the Hongzhen Fire Brigade also received the news and quickly dispatched fire trucks to the scene to put out the fire. However, by this time, the fire had become uncontrollable, and with the aid of the wind, the fire spread even more fiercely, also affecting building number 4 in Liangyi Lane. The firefighters quickly secured the lane, and surrounded the fire on all sides to extinguish it. It was not until around 2:00 AM that the fire was finally extinguished. As a result, 54 straw huts were burned down, and the disaster victims sat on the ground, homeless, exposed to the wind and cold, in a state of utter misery. Feng Zhaonian, the source of the fire, was arrested on the spot by the Fifth Precinct of the Fifth District, and taken back for interrogation. As for the cause of the fire, it was said that Feng's younger sister, Xiaolan, was playing around with someone and accidentally knocked over a kerosene lamp, and the sparks splashed onto the straw. Afterward, Feng Xiaolan fled without a trace and is now being sought.

Huang Chu Jiu's Real Estate Has Been Auctioned Off - For a Total of 227,000 Yuan 193

After the Gongfa Company Riyue Bank and the Great World Amusement Savings Department collapsed in the winter of the 19th year of the Republic due to the death of the founder, Huang Chu Jiu, owing debts of more than 3 million yuan, the creditors filed lawsuits to recover their money. Huang's family handed over all public and private property for compensation. Accountants were appointed for liquidation, and later the former French Concession Court allocated 20% of the debt. After the case was taken over by the Second Special District Court, due to the complexity of the case and the time required for the cleanup, no allocations have been made yet. Lawyers commissioned by the creditors, such as Yan Luqing, have repeatedly submitted requests for the auction of all Huang's real estate to repay the debts, as reported in previous newspapers. The court has auctioned off five properties of the debtor Gongfa Company and Huang, including the Zhizu Lu on Avenue Edward VII, the Jiufu Company at the intersection of Route Mercier and Route Park, Rongqing Lane on Route Joffre, Qiaoxi of Xicang in the city, and the Jiuzhi Xiaozhu on West Lake in Hangzhou, along with the land. They were auctioned off publicly at the execution office the other day and purchased by the wealthy merchant Li Guangdi. Together with the previous auction of six properties including the Huang Chu Jiu Hospital on Longmen Road, the total auction price was 227,000 yuan. One property, the Tongde Hospital building and land on Route de la Soeur, was originally scheduled to be auctioned on the same day, but the auction was suspended due to another lawsuit entanglement. It will be sold after the problem is resolved. At 3 PM the other day, the lawyers representing both the creditors and debtors were summoned to the court, and Judge Cao opened the court to announce the sale price, seek opinions on the allocation, and the accountant reported on the progress of the cleanup.

Zhabei - The People's Education Institute was Established Yesterday - Shi Liangcai Reported on the Founding Process 194

The Zhabei People's Education Institute, organized by the Shanghai Municipal Association, held its founding meeting at the institute's location on Liuying Road at 2 PM yesterday.

List of Guests 195

Guests included Mayor Wu Tiecheng (represented by Pan Gongzhan), Director of the Municipal Education Bureau Pan Gongzhan, as well as Shi Liangcai, Lin Kanghou, Wang Yiting, Gui Yanfang, Qian Xinzhi, Zhu Qinglan (represented by Zha Liangzhao), Chu Huiseng, Huang Renzhi, Jiang Wenyu, Wang Guanyi, Huang Jingwan, Pang Jingzhou, Xu Qianlin, Liu Wang Liming, and over a hundred others.

Interior View of Zhabei People's Education Institute (Photographed by Li Zunyong) 196

Report on the Process 197

After the meeting began, Shi Liangcai gave a report, stating roughly that after the January 28th Incident in Shanghai, the city was devastated and filled with vagrants, posing a hidden danger to the area. The gentlemen of the Shanghai Municipal Local Maintenance Association were deeply concerned and decided to establish a People's Education Institute in Zhabei to accommodate them. They allocated 100,000 yuan from the national salvation donation as a foundation. After the establishment of the Shanghai Municipal Association, they continued to prepare for the establishment, organized a board of directors, and first allocated funds to build new houses on the old site of the Zhabei Xiqin Institute. It was completed this spring. The institute had been operated by Wang Binyan and other enthusiastic charitable gentlemen in Zhabei for many years. Wang Yiting transferred 177 people from the former Hunan Temporary Shelter for the Poor, and the China Women and Children's Relief Association transferred 20 male students, together with the original residents of the Xiqin Institute, and those successively admitted to the institute, totaling over 200 people. Over the past year, there have been times of increase and decrease. As of now, there are actually 158 students in the institute. Director Zhu Yaqiang is dedicated to education and has many years of experience in administration. He studied agronomy in France and is willing to give up other careers to engage in practical work of saving people. The process of the institute's founding is roughly as described above. Next, Gao Yanyun and Gui Yanfang reported on the institute's affairs and financial situation. The speeches were omitted for length.

Pan Gongzhan's Speech 198

Next, Mayor's representative Pan Gongzhan gave a speech, saying, "Ladies and gentlemen, you have come here to attend the founding ceremony of the Education Institute, and I hope that many of you will see the desolate scene of the Eight Character Bridge, not far from here, left over from the January 28th Incident. Due to the efforts of the former Local Maintenance Association (now the Local Association), the army was supplied and refugees were accommodated during the January 28th Incident. Knowing the importance of education, this institute was established. In the past, this institute was originally a vagrant training center, because the organizers knew that the people's education was indispensable, so on the one hand, education was implemented, and on the other hand, production was implemented, so that the people could gain technical knowledge, which is more beneficial than ordinary schools. The municipal government, within the possible scope, should vigorously promote it, and hope that all sectors of the community can provide assistance. This is what the mayor instructed me to say. At the same time, I heard in the institute's song, 'Do not forget the prestige of the 19th Route Army.' However, the 19th Route Army is now pro-Japanese and tolerant of the Communists, an illegal combination, and there is no need to commemorate it any longer. I hope that the two words '19th' will be changed to 'Resist Japan,' because it was not only the 19th Route Army that resisted Japan during the Shanghai Incident. Only the army that resists Japan is worthy of commemoration, otherwise there is no need to commemorate it." Next, Liu Wang Liming gave a speech, which was not recorded due to its length. At 4:30 PM, the director led a tour of the work products of various departments, including paper boxes, bronzeware, rattan ware, woodwork, and sewing. It is said that the institute will also add an agricultural department. It was not until 5 PM that the meeting dispersed.

The houses in Mingde Lane on Avenue Joffre are the property of Chen Mingde, a Chinese, and managed by the Shanghai Bank Real Estate Department. Now the tenants are willing to increase the rent by 10%, which is already a concession. If it is necessary to

Poisoning from Eating Pufferfish Roe - Three of a Family of Five Die - Wang Changsheng and Two Children Died Tragically - His Wife Has Awakened but Her Future is Bleak 201

Wang Changsheng, a 35-year-old man from Gaoyou, had a wife, two sons, and a daughter. His wife, Tang, was 39 years old, his daughter, Fufen, was 9 years old, his son, Songyuan, was 7 years old, and his youngest son, Xiaosanzi, was only 2 years old. The family of five originally lived a very poor life by farming in their hometown. Admiring the wealth of Shanghai and the ease of making a living, they moved to Shanghai as a family in July of this year, building a reed shed on the eastern end of the Kuang Field on Dongchang Road in Pudong to live in, a very pitiful sight. Changsheng himself was not strong, and his wife and four children all depended on him for survival. He was not strong enough to do manual labor, so he had to go to the docks every day to pick up garbage or scavenge in various places to make a living. Sometimes he had nothing to gain, and the family had no food. Their inhuman life was extremely miserable. The other day in the afternoon, Changsheng again went to pick up things in the garbage bins in various alleys in Puxi. He found a string of pufferfish roe in a garbage bin near the 16th Pier, which was still very fresh. Changsheng, thinking that his family had not had any delicacies for a long time, was delighted to see it, so he took out the fish roe, brought it home, and rinsed it once. His wife had advised him to cook it tomorrow, but Changsheng was drooling and did not listen. He went to the market to buy some greens, fried tofu, and a little bit of soybeans, and cooked them with the pufferfish roe in a pot. At dinner time at around 6:00 PM that night, the family gathered together to eat it heartily. At first, they were all right, but by 9:00 or 10:00 PM, all five of them were poisoned, their bodies numb, their abdomens swollen, and they fell unconscious. Changsheng had eaten the most, so he soon died of asphyxiation. The youngest son, Xiaosanzi, had weak resistance and also died after his father. There were still three people, all on the verge of death. The neighbors immediately reported to the Third District Public Security Bureau. Chief Zhang immediately sent patrol officers to the scene and urgently carried the three dead people to the Pudong Hospital for treatment. At the same time, a bowl of uneaten pufferfish roe was found in the shed, seemingly left over for tomorrow. The police took it back to the district as evidence. After the three people arrived at the hospital, the doctor simultaneously poured medicine down their throats to make them vomit. After a long time, only Tang was able to gradually wake up. The other two children remained unconscious. Yesterday morning, the doctor saw that Tang was able to speak and immediately notified the Third District to have her carried to the district. After Chief Zhang questioned her in detail about the poisoning, seeing that Tang was out of danger, he ordered her to be carried back home. The two children in the hospital, however, because the treatment was ineffective, became even worse, so they were also sent back to their home. The nine-year-old girl, Fufen, died of asphyxiation at 3:00 PM. The seven-year-old boy, Songyuan, was also still in critical condition. After this incident occurred, it caused a sensation far and wide. The curious flocked to the mouth of the reed shed to watch, causing a huge crowd. However, the three corpses, large and small, were lying to the left and right in the shed, and one child was also unconscious. Only Tang was left alive, but when she looked back at the great disaster that had befallen her family, she also wanted to die. The scene in the small shed was extremely tragic, and the spectators were all saddened. The dead are gone, but the living not only have a worrying future, but also do not have the strength to pay for coffins and funerals. Therefore, Chief Zhang notified the charity hall to provide coffins and collect the bodies. At the same time, he instructed the neighborhood chief to report the three corpses to the court for examination.

X X X X X

Completely paying the outstanding rent, and insisting on the rent increase, truly disregard the pain of the tenants. Therefore, the tenants are preparing to resist. In addition to regularly convening meetings of all tenants to deal with the situation, they are also submitting the landlord's oppression to the party and government organs and various groups to request assistance.

Woman Attempts Suicide by Swallowing Tranquilizers 202

Ma Gao, a young woman from Wujiang, 24 years old, living at No. 16 Yuqing Lane, Triangular Vegetable Market, Zhaojia Road, City, had a quarrel with her husband, Ma Jinhai, the night before last and was beaten by Jinhai. Special Article: Preface to "Key to Understanding Characters" by Ding Fubao 209

To deeply study the writing systems of European and American countries, one must read Latin. This is because one must trace back to the origin of their character creation. If this is the case for Western writing, how could Chinese writing be any different? To trace back the construction of Chinese characters, clerical script and standard script are insufficient. One must seek the origins in seal script and bronze script to achieve true understanding. The person who compiled the great compendium of seal script, bronze script, and ancient characters was Xu Shen, during the Later Han Dynasty, in his "Shuowen Jiezi." Xie Qikun aptly said, "The 'Shuowen' is the foremost book in the world. Reading all the books in the world without reading the 'Shuowen' is equivalent to not reading at all." This is similar to saying that one who studies Western writing without reading Latin will ultimately be unable to understand the origins and development of Western writing. However, in this day and age, it is not necessary for all students to become experts in philology. It is only necessary to have a basic understanding of the errors in the transition to clerical script, the general principles of the Six Methods of Character Construction, and the construction of characters. Han Changli of the Tang Dynasty said, "Those who compose literary works should have a basic understanding of characters." This is what he meant.

However, when scholars first read the "Shuowen," they often stop halfway because the writing is ancient, obscure, dry, and uninteresting. Therefore, philologists compile the 540 radicals, adding brief annotations, or compile introductory books for beginners, or create various mnemonic verses. Although the names are numerous, the intention is to make it easier for beginners. However, readers still find it dull and uninteresting, and put it aside before finishing the book. Some are forced by strict fathers and teachers to graduate, but they find it as tasteless as chewing wax and still cannot enter the realm of philology. Why is this? It is because the compilers, although experts in Xu's scholarship, have never paid attention to what is called teaching methodology. Presuming upon myself, I intended to compile an introductory book to Xu's scholarship thirty years ago. At first, I thought it would be very easy. But as soon as I put pen to paper, it was like scooping sand from the sea, boundless and without end. Only then did I realize how difficult it was. Afterwards, I destroyed the drafts three times and revised them five times, exhausting my energy and spending my days, and still could not complete the book after more than thirty years. So, I entrusted a bundle of remaining drafts to Shen Boyuan to continue the work. After a long time, Boyuan also declined, saying that it was not easy to edit, and returned the drafts to me. They have been hidden in my trunk for another year. This autumn, Mr. Jiang Zhuzhuang said that the teachers of philology in various schools are troubled by the lack of a book that beginners can quickly use, and he urged me to complete the manuscript as soon as possible. I was not satisfied with the old drafts, so I racked my brains and searched diligently, and established a different system. Sometimes I forgot to eat while facing the food, or got up in the middle of the night. In this way, for three days and nights, I finally abandoned the old drafts and edited using the circular teaching method, naming it "Key to Understanding Characters." Alas, I am already sixty years old, and my energy is declining. This book was not completed thirty years ago, but is being completed today, in the twilight of my life. It can also be said that I do not know that old age is approaching. I especially wonder whether this will truly be a shortcut and beneficial to those who are beginning to study the "Shuowen."

At the beginning of this book is the "Preliminary Compilation." Lu Shiheng said, "Nothing is greater than words in explaining things, and nothing is better than pictures in preserving forms." I believe that when teaching beginners, words and pictures should be combined. Therefore, I have selected a number of characters, all of which are presented with illustrations to arouse interest. I imagine that at the beginning of character creation, it must have been like this. The illustrations and annotations are all taken from "Glimpses into the Six Methods" and "Elementary Steps in Philology." I hereby acknowledge this and dare not take credit for myself.

Mountain Man Luo Liangfeng painted the "Diagram of the Shuowen System" for Gui Weigu, a scholar of the Ming Dynasty, depicting eight people. The oldest is Xu Shen. Flanking him on the left and right are Jiang Shi and Yan Zhitui. Following the three sages are Li Yangbing. Those who follow behind, as if whispering together, are the Xu Xuan and Xu Kai brothers. The one dressed as a Taoist priest is Zhang You. The one with one eye and one lame foot is Wu Qiuyan (the above is from Zhang Xun's postscript). There are also inscriptions by Lu Wenchao, Wang Niansun, Zhang Xun, Weng Fanggang, Ding Jie, Gui Fu, etc. It is truly a dramatic and precious relic of historical transmission. Therefore, the portraits and the original inscriptions are all phototyped and included in the "Preliminary Compilation" so that scholars of Xu's scholarship throughout the country can see this diagram and naturally feel admiration. The original manuscript of the diagram is worth more than a thousand gold coins and is now in the possession of Mr. Zhou Meiquan. I am grateful to Mr. Zhou for generously allowing it to be printed and widely circulated. I hereby record this to ensure that I do not forget.

This book is edited using the circular teaching method and is divided into four weeks, with each week divided into five categories: 1. General Introduction to the "Shuowen": a general discussion of the outline of the "Shuowen." 2. Clerical Transformation: From seal script to clerical script, the essence of the Six Methods was almost completely destroyed. To understand the original intentions of the ancients in creating characters, one should first know the flaws of the clerical transformation. 3. The Six Methods: The Six Methods are the foundation of character creation. Indicative, pictographic, phonetic loan, and associative composition are the four forms, on which there is no disagreement. Semantic association and borrowing are the two uses, on which there are many different opinions. Here, the aim is to adopt a compromise to dispel all doubts for the reader. 4. Corner of the "Shuowen": The complete "Shuowen" has more than 9,000 characters. Here, the aim is to briefly describe the most superficial and interesting ones for the purpose of learning by analogy. 5. The Deeds of Xu Jun: to not forget one's ancestors when discussing the classics, and also as a means of discussing the world and valuing friendship.

At the end of this book is the "Postliminary Compilation," which selects the essence of various books, in three categories: 1. "Original Preface to the 'Shuowen,'" with annotations by Mr. Wang Guansan in one volume. Wang's annotations extract the best from the Duan and Gui families and have his own solid insights. It is truly the most complete commentary on Xu's preface. 2. "Preface to the Categories of the 'Shuowen'" in two volumes by Xu Cuo of the Southern Tang Dynasty, modeled after the "Preface to the Trigrams" of the "Book of Changes." It strings the "Shuowen" radicals together, deducing the reasons for the sequential generation of the 540 characters. Although there are occasional inversions, omissions, and forced interpretations, it is still a good book for reading the radicals. 3. "Inquiries into the 'Shuowen' with Corrections" in one volume by Gu Guangqi, correcting the errors in Yan Kejun's "Collated Commentary on the 'Shuowen.'" Lei Jun said that Gu's corrections are meticulously detailed, unexpected, and yet convincing, which is a fair assessment. If readers can graduate from these three, they will not only enter the gate of Xu's scholarship, but will have truly ascended to its inner chambers.

If a person's brainpower is used for the same thing for a long time, it will inevitably become tiresome. Therefore, it is advisable to change the kinds of things to relieve it. In this way, the scene will be refreshed, and the spirit of research will also be invigorated. This is why the circular teaching method was established. If the five categories in the four weeks of this book are combined class by class, each category will easily become tiresome to read and will not be able to be completed. This is why there is also the division into four weeks. Every time a scholar reads one week, he can gain considerable knowledge in five categories. By the time he finishes four weeks, he will no longer be an outsider. Moreover, there is also the mutual assistance of the "Preliminary Compilation" and "Postliminary Compilation."

The system of this book was roughly determined in three days and nights, as described above. Editing according to this should be unhindered. But who knew that there was still a major difficulty that could not be resolved, namely in the phonetic loan in the first week's "Six Methods." Xu Jun's original preface said, "Borrowing refers to those characters that originally do not exist, but rely on sound to represent things, such as 'ling' and 'zhang.'" The philologists of ancient and modern times who have discussed borrowing have numbered in the dozens, but their theories are mostly far-fetched and do not know the original meaning. Although they have constructed many betel nuts, there are more forced interpretations. In reality, no one can know Xu's meaning. I pondered and thought about it repeatedly, unable to find a definite solution. In this way, another day and night passed. Then, suddenly, I realized something and said, "I've got it! I've got it!" Zheng Kangcheng and Xu Jun were contemporaries, and his annotations to the "Three Rites" also quoted the "Shuowen." If Zheng's theories are used to understand Xu's theories, they must deeply grasp the matter. Therefore, I examined the "Preface to Explaining the Classics," which quoted Zheng's theory on borrowing, saying, "In haste, when there is no character, it is borrowed by using a similar or homophonous character, aiming to be close to it." "In haste, when there is no character" is the same as Xu's "originally there is no character." "It is borrowed by using a similar or homophonous character, aiming to be close to it" is the same as Xu's "rely on sound to represent things." Only the two characters "cu" and "ben" in clerical script are easily mistaken due to their similar forms, so "cu" was erroneously changed to "ben." For more than a thousand years, philologists have been unaware of the error in the text and have forced an explanation, resulting in increasingly complex and far-fetched theories. Now, based on Zheng's theory, it is corrected to "originally there is no character," which suddenly resonates with people's hearts. Guanzi said, "Think about it and be grateful for it, and the spirits will communicate with you." It is not the power of the spirits, but the extreme of the essence. Is this not what I am talking about today?

Mr. Wu Zhihui believes that "ling zhang" is the erroneous writing of "ling liang," and his theory is precise. The full text is detailed in the "Supplement to the Gu Lin" and in this book. It roughly says that "ling" is to issue commands. By extension, it becomes the "ling" in county magistrate, commander, to order, and laws. "Zhang" means long duration. By extension, it becomes the "zhang" in to grow, young and old, county head, and family head, all of which are semantic association. Semantic association is due to meaning, and borrowing is due to sound. The two are fundamentally different. Someone may refute this by saying, "For example, if a lecturer orally says 'county magistrate,' the scribe can write 'county head,' or if he orally says 'county head,' he can also write 'county magistrate.' Therefore, 'ling' and 'zhang' can be borrowed from each other, and it is not necessary to change it to 'ling liang.'" I say that this theory is not correct. All borrowing must be done with words that are bisyllabic, near in sound, or homophonous. Therefore, it is said that "rely on sound to represent things." "Ling" and "zhang" are not bisyllabic, near in sound, or homophonous. This is one reason why they cannot be borrowed. Examining the "Table of Officials" in the "Book of Han," counties with more than ten thousand households had magistrates, and those with less than ten thousand households had heads. According to the "Continuation of the Book of Han," each large county had one magistrate with a salary of one thousand dan of grain, and the second had a head with a salary of four hundred dan, and the small had a head with a salary of three hundred dan. The difference in the number of dan between magistrates and heads is vast. This is the second reason why they cannot be borrowed. Only "ling" and "liang," as explained in the annotations to the "Book of Poetry," both mean "good." "Ling" and "liang" are bisyllabic, so they can be borrowed from each other, such as "liang qi" which can be written as "ling qi," as in the poem "A good wife, a long-lived mother." "Liang ren" can be written as "ling ren," as in the poem "I have no good man." By attributing extension to semantic association and using similar sounds to represent things to borrowing, the boundaries between semantic association and borrowing will be clearly drawn, and the true meaning will emerge. Scholars who know this can distinguish the entanglements of ancient and modern people's theories on the Six Methods.

The difficulty of borrowing has been resolved, and the erroneous characters in Xu's preface have been corrected. Then, I began the work of editing. This book mostly adopts existing books and notes the sources to facilitate scholars' examination. Also, the layout of this book is modeled after the "Shuowen Gu Lin," because the characters are small and upright, which is convenient for students to use. If the characters are large and upright, it is not suitable. Abandoning this and taking that is my humble intention, which I hope will be deeply understood by scholars. From the beginning to the printing, it took seven months to complete. I do not dare to say that I have pioneered new paths or built new walls, but I am deeply ashamed of the delay in carving on wood and writing on paper.

Written by Ding Fubao at the Gu Lin Refined Study on November 20th, the 22nd year of the Republic of China in Wuxi.

Educational News: The Central Government Will Implement Unified Student Training in Other Cities 210

Yesterday, it was heard that the Central Government, in order to promote the firm will of young people and cultivate their integrity, ordered the Training Department of the General Staff and the Ministry of Education to jointly draft unified youth training standards for secondary and higher schools. Recent News on the Collection and Remittance of Education Fees in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province 212

The busy land tax collection in various counties of Jiangsu Province has now been uniformly changed to land price tax. Some counties have merged the busy land tax (renamed land price tax) and divided it into two phases. In addition to remitting the collected funds to the Department of Finance, the educational portion of the fees should also be remitted to the Jiangsu Education Fee Management Office. This kind of two-phase land price tax collection has some counties collecting 40% in the first phase and 60% in the second phase, while others collect 30% in the first phase and 70% in the second phase. There is also the so-called "3-3-4 system," which is divided into three phases: 30% in the first phase, 30% in the second phase, and 40% in the third phase (the former 30% in the first phase and 70% in the second phase is to merge the second phase's 30% and the third phase's 40% into one collection, which is different from the 3-3-4 system, which is collected in three phases and one in two phases). It is heard that the Department of Finance has ordered various counties to collect in two phases (40% in the first phase and 60% in the second phase) to unify the system. Various counties will have a unified approach. This busy land tax (now changed to land price tax) busy silver is collected at 1.75 yuan per tael (the education fee is 0.47 yuan). Paddy rice is collected at 2.40 yuan per shi (there are a total of 1.55 million shi in the province) by the Department of Finance and 1.60 yuan by the education fee, totaling (the so-called land tax) over two million yuan of education fees annually. The Education Fee Management Office is worried that various counties will divert funds. In addition to areas with inconvenient transportation or where the number of education fees is too small to conveniently send a special commissioner to manage the allocation in the county, most of the counties in Jiangnan and the larger counties in Jiangbei have separately allocated education fees and deposited them in the treasury, with special commissioners in charge. Currently, there are more than 30 counties that have been allocated. The performance of these allocated counties in collecting and remitting educational special funds is relatively good, and many unallocated counties are also doing their best to collect and remit education fees. It is also heard that Jiangning Experimental County has increased its tax revenue several times since handling land reporting and clearing up long-standing abuses. The number of education fees has therefore increased unprecedentedly, but the county government has already stored these education fees separately and has not yet remitted them to the Education Fee Management Office.

French Novelist de Guérande Departs from Beiping for Japan; Believes that the Beauty of China is Like the Magic of a Beautiful Woman; This Trip is Not a Farewell, and He Will Return to China After Traveling in Japan 213

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) French novelist de Guérande will leave Beiping for Tianjin tomorrow (the 17th) and then travel to Japan. He will return to China in the future for an in-depth tour. The reporter visited Mr. de at the Beijing Hotel today (the 16th) and was received. Here are the key points of his conversation: Before leaving Beiping, I would like to talk to the reporter. Beiping is like a large park, enough to evoke my memories of Versailles. Versailles is the old capital of France, the place where the king lived. Since the revolution of 1789, the capital has moved. My love for Beiping is like my love for Versailles. Every stone and every house in Beiping can prove that it has been the center of prosperity for thousands of years. After traveling in Japan, I plan to return to China for about four or five months, so that I can travel all over South China and the major ports in the Yangtze River basin, and finally to Yunnan. The second time I go to China, I will first visit Beiping. There are four major cities in the world: New York, Paris, Venice, and Beiping, each with its own unique style. Those with a poetic soul cannot forget the beauty of Beiping. I hope that Beiping will never be destroyed by modern Europeans, and even building tall Western-style buildings is inferior to this natural beauty with poetic flavor. Another sight of Beiping is the hutongs. No one can imagine that there are still such artistic families in the hutongs. After returning to China from Japan and arriving in Shanghai, I hope to visit the local film factories. Therefore, this temporary farewell is not a farewell to China, because I will still return to China. The beauty of China is like the magic of a beautiful woman. If someone rejects this magic, they will definitely regret it ten thousand years later. I plan to write two novels based on my impressions of traveling in China and will begin writing after leaving China.

Ministry of Education Inspector Gu Zhaolin Returns to Beijing After Inspection; Discusses the Educational Situation in Suiyuan, Chahar, and Shanxi 214

Gu Zhaolin, an inspector of the Ministry of Education, inspected education in Suiyuan, Chahar, and Shanxi provinces for a period of 53 days. He has now completed his work and returned to the ministry on the 14th to work. His inspection report is being compiled in detail. Based on his private conversations, the educational situation in these three provinces is briefly described below:

Suiyuan It is reported that Inspector Gu visited Gui Sui (Guihua City and Suiyuan City are about three miles apart) and Baotou. Before the 13th year of the Republic of China, Suiyuan only had one school, the First Middle School. In the 14th year of the Republic of China, during the Northwest Army era, the original Five Ethnicities Academy was changed to Zhongshan Academy, gradually promoting education. Now there are two male normal schools, one female normal school, two middle schools, one Zhongshan Academy, one vocational school, and one private middle school. The general situation of school education: The First Middle School has been established for the longest time, and the school site is sufficient, but the equipment is slightly simple. The First Normal School is not in Guihua City, but in the Palace Lord's Mansion, which is very large and has old-style palace houses, and new buildings have been built recently, but the equipment also feels simple. The Vocational School and Zhongshan Academy are both in Suiyuan City, and the school site is sufficient. The Vocational School has agricultural vocational subjects and the equipment is insufficient, so the equipment of scientific instruments and specimens in various schools in Suiyuan is insufficient, which is a common shortcoming. In terms of education, there have been student movements in recent years, and students cannot concentrate on studying, but the students are very honest and hardworking. The school spirit is not good, which is caused by local factions using students. In terms of funding, the province's education expenditure (including social education and elementary schools) is 270,000 yuan, with secondary education accounting for 180,000 yuan. There is also an education fund, which is a 20% surcharge on special taxes, with 70,000 yuan per year used as temporary expenses, so various schools are still able to engage in construction and equipment. The education fee has a partial independence, and the financial authorities are willing to designate several types of funds for the complete independence, but the education sector is afraid to accept it because there is no fixed and guaranteed source of funds in Suiyuan. Therefore, it is difficult for education fees to be completely independent for a while. The subsequent plan has been discussed by the inspector of the Ministry of Education and the educational administrative authorities of Suiyuan, and it has been generally agreed to change Zhongshan Academy into a vocational school and expand the original vocational school. It is estimated that by the 26th year of the Republic of China, the vocational school's funding will reach the standard of 35% of secondary education funding. The reorganization plan of the vocational school has not yet been determined, but it generally tends to focus on the local specialties and needs, such as wool weaving and livestock improvement.

Chahar It is reported that Inspector Gu inspected Zhangjiakou and Xuanhua. Chahar Province originally had one agricultural college, but this year it stopped recruiting college students (because the school's facilities are not sufficient to recruit college students) and instead recruited common middle school students. There are two normal schools and two female normal schools, as well as two middle schools, one vocational school, and one private middle school. The general situation is that the normal school has the most funding, and the vocational school has the least. According to the current financial situation, it is not easy for funding to be independent. Xuanhua School is very large in scale and has impressive equipment. The school buildings in Zhangjiakou, except for the agricultural college built by Feng Huanzhang in Xin Village with a subsidy of 10,000 yuan from the provincial government, are all rented from private houses, which are mostly not applicable. The general equipment of various schools is acceptable, but the scientific instrument equipment is lacking. The subsequent plan is to convert the original college into a vocational school, merge the original two normal schools into one, and keep one of the original two female normal schools and convert the other into a female middle school. There will be slight changes in the middle school. The implementation of this plan is estimated to reach the standard of 40% of secondary school funding by the 26th year of the Republic of China.

Shanxi Inspector Gu inspected Datong, Daixian, Taiyuan, and Changzhi (the former capital of Lu'an Prefecture). The province has colleges above the specialty, including Shanxi University with three colleges of arts, law, and engineering, which has a long history. There are also two provincial law colleges and education colleges. Specialty schools include three specialty schools for agriculture, industry, and commerce. The private Binzhou University has not yet been registered. There is also the private Chuan Zhi Medical College, founded by Yan Xishan. Shanxi University has three colleges of arts, law, and engineering, and there are two provincial law colleges and education colleges, with overlapping departments. The last time Inspector Dai of the Ministry of Education inspected the results, the Ministry of Education ordered the two provincial law and education colleges to be merged into Shanxi University, but this has not yet been implemented. The biggest two reasons are (1) the department order arrived when the examination was being held, and (2) the funding standards are different. After the merger, the provincial treasury must add funding (Shanxi University's education fee is 16 yuan per point, and the law and education colleges are 12 yuan per point. After the merger, it must be 16 yuan uniformly). Many of the province's vocational schools have affiliated high schools. There are many private high schools in Taiyuan City, which can be said that Shanxi's high schools are concentrated in Taiyuan. Because of this situation, students graduating from junior high school can only enter high school except for normal school, and high school graduates must enter colleges above the specialty. Because there are more places for humanities and science departments in provincial and private schools, they can only enter the humanities and science departments. After graduation, because of what they have learned, they are mostly engaged in humanities and science matters. There are more than 1,500 university students in public and private universities, with 300 to 400 graduates each year, and it is already difficult to find a way out. There is one national normal school, five provincial schools, and five provincial female normal schools. Normal school education fees account for 57% of secondary school education, and Shanxi is the province with the most popular compulsory education. There are a population of 300,000 in Taiyuan City, and only 1,000 children are out of school, but according to the current situation, the training of teachers already exceeds the demand. Originally, there were no high schools in various places outside the province, whether provincial or county, only junior high schools. This year, three high school classes were newly recruited in Datong, Yuncheng, and Ningwuguan, so people seeking high school education in various places have equal opportunities, but there are still many private high schools in Taiyuan Province, so there are quite a lot of students. The province's education fees are more than 1.9 million yuan, and are currently issued at 80% of the discount and have not yet been independent. Originally, there were three agricultural vocational schools. This year, a new livestock vocational school and a salt affairs vocational school were established. The funding for these five secondary vocational schools accounts for only 3% of the funding, and efforts will be made to promote them in the future. The overall education plan for the province has been agreed upon in principle by the provincial administrative authorities and the inspector of the ministry, and will be announced after being approved by the ministry.

Second Jiangsu Province Normal Education District Education Improvement Association Holds 3rd Congress in Wujiang 215

(Suzhou Dispatch) The Second Jiangsu Province Normal Education District Education Improvement Association held its third congress on the 16th in Wujiang. Over fifty representatives from education bureaus and member schools of the ten counties of Wuxian, Wujiang, Changshu, Wujin, Yixing, Jingjiang, Liyang, Jiangyin, Wuxi, and Jintan attended. The exhibition focused on educational administration achievements, and the research scope was labor education. Automobiles on the Su-Jia Road chartered a special car to transport members. Local elementary schools in this county also sent achievement products to participate. It was truly a grand event.

The achievement exhibition began at 8:30 AM. Five exhibition venues were opened simultaneously: (1) Wujiang Rural Normal School - First venue, displaying exhibits from member schools. The Suzhou Central Normal Department had no exhibits. The Luoshe Rural Normal School's charts and diagrams were novel. (2) Executive Committee, and recommended the Huangdu Rural Normal School and others to sort out the proposals. In the afternoon, at the second venue, the Rural Normal School Affiliated Elementary School, exhibits from member schools were displayed. Jiangyin Rural Normal School, Jingjiang Rural Normal School, and Jingjiang Rural Normal School Affiliated Elementary School had no exhibits. (3) Wujiang Middle School - Third venue, displaying exhibits from county education bureaus and local elementary schools. Wujin County had no achievements. Wuxi Education Bureau had dozens of items. Changshu Education Bureau and Shishi and Shimei Elementary Schools had approximately two hundred items. (4) Chengzhong Elementary School served as the fourth venue, displaying exhibits from local elementary schools, with Wujiang having the most. Jintan only had sixteen items. Liyang, Jingjiang, Jiangyin, and Yixing each had empty rooms. (5) Chengxi Elementary School displayed Wuxian's achievements, occupying seven rooms two thirds full, with a total of over seven thousand items, making it the most notable location for representatives from various counties.

The opening ceremony was at 9:00 AM. The congress held the opening ceremony in the Dacheng Hall of Wujiang. The ceremony was performed as usual. Standing Committee member Shen Peixian reported that the political situation had changed repeatedly in recent years, but the theory of labor education had not changed. On the contrary, its importance had increased. Since American scholars advocated for it after the May Fourth Movement, countries such as Soviet Russia and Slavic countries have adapted successively, achieving good results. It is necessary to implement labor education for the sake of both private morality and saving expenses. The scope of discussion at this congress is based on this. Then Zhang Beihu reported on the preparations, saying that holding the congress in Wujiang was truly embarrassing, because Wujiang City is not even as good as a rural village. In terms of food, lodging, and transportation, the hotel could not simultaneously provide meals for more than twenty people. The entire city's inns only had about twenty beds. There were also few bus routes. Therefore, a preparatory meeting was reopened on the 13th to remedy the situation. Furthermore, the originally designated two school buildings for the achievement exhibition suddenly received a telegram from Wuxian requesting four more rooms. At that time, there was great panic, because one county required four rooms, and ten counties would need four rooms each. Unfortunately, all the elementary and middle schools in the city only had over twenty classrooms, which was truly difficult. Now, fortunately, things were barely managed. The preparatory committee expressed its deep apologies to all members.

Celebrity Speech: The congress appointed Xishi, Wujiang Education Bureau, and Wujiang Rural Normal School as the presidium. Then celebrity Tao Xingzhi was invited to give a speech titled "A Lecture on Labor Education." After the speech, eleven local groups in Wujiang held a public banquet for all members in the Minglun Hall.

Key Resolutions: At 2:00 PM, the Education Improvement Association held a research conference. The presidium, Shen Peixian, Zhang Beihu, and Jin Shuqiao, reported that today's discussion on the scope of labor education is limited to elementary schools. The discussion included: (1) Changshu Education Bureau's proposal to abolish labor as a separate subject and implement laborization in all subjects was resolved to be retained. (2) Wujiang Rural Normal School's proposal to develop elementary school labor subject teaching materials: (1) Urban elementary schools should focus on simple industry. The teaching material outline should include clothing cutting and sewing, weaving of clothes and socks, bleaching and dyeing of cloth threads, making and bleaching of grass mats, making of rattan chairs and tables, making and polishing methods of simple woodworking tools, methods of silvering and nickel plating, manufacturing of tooth powder, painting of simple utensils, manufacturing of soap, manufacturing of candles, manufacturing of dry batteries, ordering of lecture notes, printing, making of toothbrushes, making of chicken feather dusters, tying of potted landscapes, manufacturing of simple bamboo crafts, making of paper flowers, sculpting of clay figures, making of paper fans, making of fly swatters, making of mosquito incense, and repairing of electric lamps. (2) Rural elementary schools should focus on agriculture. The teaching material outline should include tilling, weeding, sowing, transplanting, harvesting, irrigating, fertilizing, pest control, seed selection, grafting, pruning, raising livestock, manufacturing of simple agricultural tools, manufacturing of simple agricultural products, plastering walls, paving floors, building roads, weaving fences, making straw sandals, making raincoats, making bamboo hats, making silkworm rearing tools, raising silkworms, making seeds, pruning mulberry trees, beekeeping, harvesting honey, grinding tofu, making broomcorns, and knitting fishing nets. Is this appropriate? Please decide. Resolved: To be submitted to the Real Elementary School Federation for discussion and revision. (3) Wujiang Education Bureau's proposal on how to promote labor teaching was resolved: (1) To collect implementation methods of labor education from various schools. (2) To open a labor subject training institute during the summer vacation next year. (3) To hold a labor subject achievement exhibition in the next academic year. (4) To have the Affiliated Elementary School of Xishi responsible for compiling and printing a special issue on labor education, and to have various schools send their implementation results to the Education Department for publication in "Elementary School Teachers" at any time. (5) To separately identify the responsible schools for implementation projects. School affairs are to be undertaken by Suzhou Central Real Elementary School and Wujiang Rural Normal School. Home affairs are to be undertaken by Suzhou Women's Normal School, Wujin Women's Normal School, and the Affiliated Elementary School of Wujiang Rural Normal School. Agricultural arts are to be undertaken by Luoshe Rural Normal School, the Affiliated Elementary School of Luoshe Rural Normal School, and Changshu Rural Normal School. Industrial arts are to be undertaken by Wuxian Rural Normal School and Xishi, and the Affiliated Elementary School of Xishi will undertake all projects. (4) Suzhou Central Real Elementary School's proposal on how labor education can achieve production goals was resolved: (1) To eliminate fine work such as cutting, pasting, and threading paper from labor subjects in middle and upper grades, and instead focus on productive, economical, and practical work. (2) To fully educate children in labor skills of investigation, research, practice, farming, animal husbandry, and local industry. (3) To have children do direct productive labor during their spare time. (4) Schools should do their best to equip larger farms and various labor tools. (5) The industrial arts curriculum in normal schools should focus on productive labor training. (5) Suzhou Central Real Elementary School's proposal to guide children in implementing family labor was resolved: (1) Schools should investigate the family environment of each child and formulate family labor courses, providing separate guidance for implementation. (2) Teachers should critique labor achievements. School labor and family labor should each account for a considerable score. (3) Family labor competitions should be held at any time, such as crop achievement competitions and chicken raising competitions. (6) Wujiang Education Bureau's proposal that rural elementary schools should give priority to adding agricultural fields to the labor subject was resolved: The association should submit a request to the Education Department to order the education bureaus of various counties in the district to order rural elementary schools to add agricultural practice fields and agricultural equipment in the shortest possible time. (7) Changshu Education Bureau's proposal on what method should be used to examine students' home affairs and agricultural affairs achievements to obtain accurate results was resolved: To use questionnaire surveys and achievement exhibitions, or achievement competitions. (8) Should labor education teaching materials be different depending on gender? Resolved: Girls' schools should follow the regulations of the Ministry of Education and apply labor appropriate for girls' schools. For co-educational schools, there is no need to differentiate. (9) Wujin Women's Normal School and Wujiang Rural Normal School's proposal on how labor education should be implemented in schools without agricultural or industrial fields was resolved: Schools should use the nearby environment to remedy the situation. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM and was scheduled to continue the next day.

Jiangsu Third District Elementary School Education Research Association Holds Meeting 216

The founding congress of the Jiangsu Province Third District Elementary School Education Research Association and the third congress of the Third District Normal Education Improvement Research Association were held simultaneously on the 15th of this month at the Kunshan County Education Bureau.
