Published every Monday, Issue 53

Economic System and Economic Society by Tang Kun 269

In today's economic society, anyone who wants to understand the Chinese economic situation is relentlessly cursing capitalist economics. They curse capitalism as a demon that sucks human blood. Moreover, the capitalist economy is especially strongly opposed by the Chinese scholar-official class, because China is currently a defeated member under the economic invasion of capitalist countries. The reason for this is China's own lack of vigor and the wrong foundation laid on its own national base. Any production technology in China is inferior to other countries. In the United States, Japan, and England, because of the development of capitalist countries, they spare no national spirit to seek the markets of other countries where capitalism is based (explicitly speaking, it is a position for exploitation); even to the point of conflicting with other countries for interests, causing military confrontation. Observing the war clouds spreading across the Pacific, Japan, the United States, Russia, and England are all sharpening their swords, preparing for another world war for the sake of their own country's capitalist needs. At the same time, the center of the war problem caused by capitalist countries seizing markets will soon be our Far East; and this place is still our China. The reason for this is that China's own production technology is not sophisticated, and the population is large, holding the helm of the world; because of the large population, the social consumption capacity also increases accordingly. Under this phenomenon, capitalist countries with overproduction are most coveted; and become the market that must be occupied for capitalist invasion. At the same time, the corruption of China's internal affairs and the frequency of banditry make all capitalist countries regard it as meat on the chopping board. Because of this, China's curse on capitalism is not absolutely without reason. With this kind of reason for opposition, there has been a tendency towards socialism in the recent Chinese economic circles; but whether China needs a socialist economic system now; or whether this socialist economy can be achieved in China, is a big question. The reason is that China's economic society has never been organized. You cannot say that it is a capitalist economy or society; nor can you say that it is a socialist economic society. China's current economic system and economic society are completely a backward member who cannot keep up with the new economic thinking. In England, the United States, and other countries, they have a large number of factories; from these factories, they can have a large amount of production; regardless of whether this large amount of production is needed or not by the economic society, the conditions that they can create for capitalism cannot be denied. In Soviet Russia, the economic organization is fully trending towards a socialist economic system. It can statistically manage various factories under the jurisdiction of the government. All production and economic relations with the country can be relaxed or tightened under the government's leadership. As for our China? Is it really a joke to say that it is a capitalist country? Not only has it lost the large number of factories needed to invade the economic markets of other countries; its own factories are still very immature, under the dangerous situation of other capitalist countries. At the same time, other capitalist countries are still trying their best to invade our market. In a corner of the Shanghai concession, factories of various countries stand in great numbers, and the outflow of annual rights is unknown how much; then this situation is certainly not a capitalist country; and it cannot be denied that China is now a pitiful worm suffering from the losses of capitalist countries. As for the socialist country? It seems that China does not have a country with a socialist economic organization. Politically, it lacks a strong and powerful government; and the government's ability to lead. Economically, it lacks a large number of factories in the country that can provide for the consumption of those countrymen; then what kind of economic system and economic society is China? This question seems to be a difficult one. Naturally, the capitalist system is impossible in China; and at the same time, it is not possible; and further, even if it could, it would create more unemployed workers and much more chaotic social data than any other country. As for the socialist economic system? There is indeed some trend in the current remarks of Chinese economists; but whether it is possible is a question. Of course, the change of the economic system is not a matter of a day or two; it is useless to simply sing high-profile tunes. To study this question, we only need to ask ourselves when China can implement a socialist economy. Naturally, it is impossible for China to talk about any kind of economic organization now, because China is now a country with backward production technology; at the same time, the internal affairs of the country cannot be unified, bandits are rampant, and the oppression of the great powers, like prisoners wearing fetters, is trapped in a semi-colonial state. If everyone wants to seek the lowest living standard; it is still impossible in fact. The main reason for this is that the creation of an economic organization completely holds a large number of factories; and a large amount of production, as well as the tools to exploit the economic markets of other countries; in China, none of these exist, so if China wants to create a socialist economic organization, the first step is to develop its own production, so that the Chinese people can each be self-sufficient. At the same time, internally, it must not be so scattered, because under the current economic situation in China, the products of this place are often unable to accommodate that place; just imagine that there is such a gap in the country itself, and you want to realize the socialist economic organization just by holding an idea, of course, it is no different from dreaming. However, the economic trend in China cannot conceal that it is trending towards the road of socialism. The statistics of various industries in the country; the inability to improve economic technology, are all showing everywhere that China is gradually moving towards the road of socialism. We do not want to say prophetic words here, we only pray for success for any kind of system at present.

Currency War Among England, America, and France by Zhao Chaogou 270

The modern economic organization is based on currency, and the fluctuation of currency value is enough to determine the trend of the economic world. The masters of the world's currency are the US dollar, the British pound, and the French franc. Currently, it is an era of melee among these three currencies. The smile or frown of these three currencies is a factor that dominates the economies of various countries; the destination of these three currencies is also the destination of the world economy. Therefore, in order to understand the world economy, we cannot ignore the actions of these three, and through these three, we can also glimpse a side of the world economy.

But although it is said to be a melee of three currencies, we must examine them separately. The first culprit in the war is the US dollar. On the battlefield, it is the active one. If it is willing to be stable, the stability of the pound and the franc is not a problem. Although England belongs to the ranks of suspending the gold standard, it has long hoped for exchange rate stability. The Exchange Equalisation Account is to prevent the pound from rising, but it also prevents the pound from falling too much. However, if the United States actively challenges, it will naturally come out to respond. The most suffering is the franc. France, which is free within the gold standard system, cannot resist by lowering the exchange rate. It has to defend itself with tariffs and other methods. Needless to say, it does not have the ability to counterattack. Whether it can resist the double attack of the United Kingdom and the United States is still a question.

X X X

The goal of the US currency policy is to increase prices. After Roosevelt inflated the currency, it initially had a considerable effect on prices, but after August, a reaction occurred again, and stock prices gradually fell. Then he decided to use a new currency policy, that is, to purchase gold at home and abroad. According to Roosevelt's statement, he wanted to raise prices to a considerable level, and then stabilize the value of the US dollar. To achieve this goal, it is necessary for the government to buy gold and lower the US dollar. According to the US currency law, one ounce of gold is equal to 20.67 yuan. The price at which the government buys gold is above the par value. The gold purchase price on October 25 was 31.36 yuan per ounce, which was 34% higher than the par value.

However, whether purchasing gold to increase prices can achieve the goal is still a question. If you want gold to be expensive to suppress the US dollar price, thereby increasing prices, you must consider two different situations. If the European gold standard group can continue to exist, the decline in exchange rates can indeed stimulate the rise in prices. But if the European gold standard group collapses and abandons the full gold standard system, the US dollar will have the risk of becoming expensive. Judging from the objective situation, if the US insists on its gold purchase policy, the abandonment of the gold standard by the gold standard group is always inevitable. However, the United States is not without considering this point. The United States is hoping that France will abandon the gold standard in order to inflate the currency of the world. After the United States suspended the gold standard, the rate of price increase has already surpassed the rate of exchange rate decline (the price index in July was 103, which was 28% higher than in March, and the US dollar in July only fell by 22%). The decline in prices after August was mostly due to the response of prices to the exchange rate. Therefore, if the United States continues to raise prices, it must try its best to lower the value of the US dollar. For this reason, it cannot take care of other issues.

X X X

After the United States announced the purchase of gold on October 29, it seemed to have thrown a bomb on the world financial market. If you buy gold domestically, although the US dollar will fall, it will only cause unrest to the currencies of other countries. Once you buy overseas gold, not only will the US dollar fall, but also the cash of various countries will concentrate in the United States, which will fundamentally harm the financial markets of various countries. Let us look at the trend of the Anglo-American exchange rate and gold price before and after the US bought gold:

Date British Gold Price US Gold Price Anglo-American Exchange Rate

Shilling Yuan

October 24 128.01 29.80 4.7725

October 25 130.01 31.36 4.7325

November 1 131.09 32.26 4.80125

November 2 133.03 32.36 4.845

November 3 133.02 32.57 4.84125

November 4 132.04 32.67 4.8625

November 5 131.10 32.84 4.8925

November 6 129.11 32.84 4.91

The US gold purchase price on October 25 was 31.36 yuan, which was 1.56 yuan higher than on October 24. After that, it gradually increased, and the Anglo-American exchange rate also gradually rose. On November 5, it exceeded the old par value of 4.87, and it was rumored that the Anglo-American exchange rate ratio was established. It was confirmed to be inaccurate on the 6th. The US gold price was 33.05 yuan, and the Anglo-American exchange rate was 4.97 yuan. The exchange rate the day before yesterday (December 5) was still above the par value (5.12 yuan).

From the British point of view, the pound is expensive. The expensive pound can make the British currency contract, the industry shrink, and unemployment increase, which is exactly what Britain cannot tolerate. The tool for Britain to control the exchange rate is the Exchange Equalisation Account. If the pound continues to be expensive, Britain will definitely use the Equalisation Account to lower it. In this way, there will be a competition between England and the United States. On October 27, the US purchase price was 31.76, which was equal to 135 shillings and two pence for British gold. The London gold price was lower than 131 shillings and two pence, with a difference of four shillings. In this situation, if the United Kingdom does not raise the gold price, the London gold market will be completely absorbed. This forces the United Kingdom to follow the same path as the United States, reduce the pound price, and inflate the currency.

X X X

The pound and the US dollar have both performed a tragic drama of falling. Whether the franc can avoid this tragedy is quite hypothetical. We know that the most difficult position after the US bought gold is undoubtedly France. The United Kingdom has suspended the gold standard and can use the Exchange Equalisation Account to lower the pound. France still adheres to the gold standard and can never autonomously lower the value of the franc. France has an annual deficit budget of 10 billion francs and an annual trade surplus of about 10 billion francs. Although the reserves are very sufficient, for the benefit of the national economy, it seems that it is necessary to abandon the gold standard. A fiscal deficit of 10 billion francs and a trade surplus of 10 billion francs are enough to shake the foundation of the franc. Even a 100% reserve is difficult to be a barrier under the US gold purchase policy. Let us look at the gold prices in New York and Paris on October 28:

New York 31.8 yuan

Paris 30.8 yuan

The difference between them is one yuan. The Atlantic gold wheel shipping fee is only six cents per ounce of US dollar. Under such a difference, can the reserves of the Bank of France still be maintained?

The US gold purchase policy can never be suspended temporarily, and the extent of the US dollar's decline has not yet reached its limit, because the United States has not yet reached the lowest standard of currency value. This can be inferred from the following table and standards:

US Dollar Gold Amount Exchange Rate Decline Rate Gold Price Gold Price Increase Percentage

A Legal Par Value 23.2|| 20.7 ||

B 100 Francs = 6 Yuan 15.235 31.6 53

C Minimum Limit Reduced by the National Farmers Conference 15.5 43 36.2 75

D President's Reduction Authority 11.6 50 41.4 100

According to the above table, the current US currency value is only at the B stage. According to the recent situation, the United States is proceeding towards the CD two stages. If the US dollar falls into the CD two stages, the difference between the gold prices in New York and Paris will be as high as five or six yuan. If France does not suspend the gold standard, how can it prohibit the outflow of gold?

The franc is not only subject to the frontal attack of the US dollar, but also the side attack of the British pound. If the United Kingdom fixes the Anglo-French exchange rate at a price of one pound for 80 francs, then when the US dollar enters the CD two stages, the Anglo-American exchange rate will fall to 5.59 or 6.31 yuan, which is definitely not what the United Kingdom wants. For its own sake, the United Kingdom has to leave the franc and follow the US dollar, using the Equalisation Account to stabilize the Anglo-American exchange rate, then when the US dollar reaches the CD two stages, the Anglo-French exchange rate will fall to 70 francs or 62 francs. In this way, the franc is also oppressed by the British pound.

The double attack of the US dollar and the British pound will inevitably make the trend of France's trade deficit more serious, international lending worse, and the domestic economy shrink. In this way, it is necessary to suspend the gold standard.

Yang Xianxu on Social Insurance in Soviet Russia 271

The social insurance system in Soviet Russia is based on the Labor Law passed in 1922, which came into effect on November 15 of that year. It also applies to other republican nations within the Union. Initially, social insurance only covered workers facing physical danger, but in 1930, unemployed individuals also became eligible. The administration of this system is entirely in the hands of the Trade Union Federation, with funding coming from individual workers. I will now discuss the scope, administration, funding sources, and distribution methods of the program.

(1) Scope of the Program: Social insurance has a broad scope, covering all wage-earning workers regardless of their length of employment, nature of work, or method of compensation. However, the implementation of old-age pensions was slower and phased in gradually. The textile industry had it in 1927, while other basic industries began issuing them in 1929. By 1932, all industries were issuing pensions, except for temporarily employed workers. The number of insured individuals from 1924 to 1932 is shown in the table below:

Year　Number of Insured People

1925　6,700,000

1926　8,200,000

1927　9,000,000

1928　9,700,000

1929　10,500,000

1930　12,700,000

1931　17,150,000

1932　20,700,000

The number of insured people increased from 6.7 million in 1925 to 20.7 million in 1932, more than tripling in just a few years, which is a remarkably rapid development. (2) Administrative Overview: The characteristics of the Soviet social insurance administration include using the same methods for various risks, and the special relationship between fund management and the Trade Union Federation. Before 1931, all administrative functions were handled by committees composed of representatives elected by the Trade Union Federation. The funds were shared by various industries in a region, with only transportation workers insured by their industry's fund. However, after 1931, this regional organizational system underwent major reforms. To promote economic recovery and the various industries included in the Five-Year Plan, industry-specific funds were established, such as those for the copper and iron industry, machinery industry, coal mining industry, oil industry, chemical industry, and transportation industry. Workers in other industries were still covered by regional industry funds. On June 23 of this year, the Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union issued an order to completely abolish all regional funds, and the administration of insurance programs was entrusted to the Central Committee of the Trade Union Federation and its affiliated commercial organizations. In 1931, the seven industry-specific insurance funds covered over 5,316,000 workers. Although the number of regional industry funds decreased from 634 in 1924 to 401 in 1929, it gradually increased thereafter. In 1932, there were a total of 3,209 funds, including 1,147 industry-specific funds and 2,062 regional industry funds. The number of insured people reached 6,912,810, with 3,458,169 belonging to industry-specific insurance funds and 3,458,641 belonging to regional insurance funds.

(3) Sources of Funding: Funding comes from contributions from individual workers. The contribution rates differ between general workers and farmers, and among general workers, there are three different rates:

(1) Ordinary Rate: Applies to general businesses and those without specific rates. It is further divided into four categories based on the degree of risk in various businesses: 16% of wages for the first category, 18% for the second, 20% for the third, and 22% for the fourth. (2) Preferential Rate: Applies to workers in agencies funded by local or national expenditures, as well as postal and telecommunications services and state farms. This is further divided into three categories: 10% of wages for the first category, 12% for the second, and 14% for the third. (3) Special Rate: Applies to various construction businesses, etc. As for the contribution rates for farmers, they are divided into three categories based on economic and social conditions: 22% for middle peasants, 10% for collective farms, and 6% for poor peasants. In addition to contributing to the insurance fund, employees also contribute to a housing construction fund (at a rate of 0.76% to 1.65%) and a fund for training construction personnel.

The following table shows the total amount of these funds and the amount available for distribution per insured person from 1925 to 1931:

Year　Total Funds (Millions of Rubles)　Distribution Amount (Rubles)

1925　474.2　70.78

1926　703.4　85.78

1927　923.2　102.58

1928　1,050.2　182.85

1929　1,258.8　119.89

1930　1,796.0　141.42

1931　3,463.3　143.63

The figures for 1931 are only for the first nine months. The estimated amount for 1932 is 3.534 billion rubles, and the projected amount for 1933 is 4.431 billion.

(4) Insurance Benefits: Insurance benefits are available in the following situations: (1) Temporary or permanent loss of work capacity due to work-related injuries. (2) Old age and infirmity. (3) Death. (4) Unemployment.

Insurance benefits are not only provided in cash but also in kind, including medical supplies provided by the health committees of the seven republican nations within the Union. All insured persons, those without working ability, the elderly, and their families are eligible. The expenses are partly funded by the state and local sources, and there are also provisions for hospitals, maternity care, and appropriate food. The following table shows these expenses and their sources since 1930 (in millions of rubles):

Total Expenses for Medical Care, etc.　Percentage of Total Expenditure　Amount Drawn from Insurance Fund

1930　997　33.5　334.0

1931　1,306　39.1　510.0

1932　1,916　40.3　772.5

Cash benefits are provided according to the following conditions: (1) Temporary Loss of Work Capacity: Initially, those who temporarily lost their work capacity were paid their full wages during the period of inability to work. After 1929, this was slightly modified based on the nature of their industry and the length of their service in that industry. For example, workers in social services who have worked in the industry for more than three years receive full wages from the first day. Workers in industry and transportation only receive three-quarters of their wages for the first five days, and full wages from the sixth day onward. As for women who cannot work due to pregnancy and childbirth, they are paid their full wages for eight weeks before and after childbirth.

(2) Additional Benefits: There are three additional benefits: A. Women receive a maternity allowance during the maternity period. In 1932, the amount of the allowance ranged from 16 to 30 rubles depending on the location. After 1932, the minimum was set at 32 rubles. B. Nursing expenses are provided for a certain period. Before 1932, 4 to 8 rubles were given per month for nine months. Later, it was changed to a one-time payment of 45 rubles. C. Funeral expenses: A funeral allowance of 21 to 45 rubles is provided after the death of an insured person, depending on the location of death. However, after 1932, it was uniformly set at 40 rubles in cities and 20 rubles in rural areas.

(3) Permanent Loss of Work Capacity: Those who permanently lose their work capacity can be divided into three categories based on the degree of loss: the first category includes those who have completely lost their capacity and require care; the second category includes those who have completely lost their capacity and cannot work in their original industry or in other industries; and the third category includes those who cannot work in their original industry but still have some capacity to do some work or other easier tasks. Before 1932, work-related accidents resulting in the third category were the most common, while the first two categories were less common. However, after 1932, these three categories were completely abolished and replaced with the following two:

A. Those who cannot work due to reasons other than work-related accidents: In 1932, the amount of subsidies for this type of situation depended on the degree of loss of capacity, the amount of wages in their industry, and the circumstances of their place of residence. Since 1932, the amount of subsidies has been changed to depend on the importance of the insured person's position in the industry and the length of their service in that industry. For example, a worker who loses work capacity while working in the mining industry can receive 69% (the highest) of their original wage, and an additional 2% is added because they have served in the industry for more than ten years. (From ten to eighteen years, an additional 12% is added; from eighteen to twenty-three years, an additional 3% is added.) In total, they can receive 71% of their original wage. If they lose part of their work capacity and have served for more than eighteen years, they can receive 30% of their original wage, plus an additional 0.5% per year (from eighteen years onwards, an additional 0.5% is added for each year of service up to thirty-four years). Therefore, the maximum amount they can receive is 41% of their original wage. XXB. Those who cannot work due to work-related accidents: Before 1932, they were given 10% to 100% of their original wage. However, after that, those who have lost their work capacity and require care are given the full amount of their original wage. Those who have only lost all or part of their capacity are treated the same as those who cannot work due to non-work-related accidents. (4) Old-Age Pensions: Old-age pensions are granted to men who have served for 25 years and are over 60 years old, and to women who have served for 20 years and are over 55 years old. In 1932, old-age pensions ranged from 50% to 100% of the original wage, depending on the location. Since 1932, this has been changed to 50% to 60% of the original wage, depending on the industry of the insured person.

(5) Survivor Benefits: Survivor benefits should be provided to the families of workers who die from non-work-related accidents. In cities, one-third or three-quarters of the original wage is given depending on the number of applicants. In rural areas, 5.5 to 28 rubles are given per month, depending on the number of applicants. Since 1932, this survivor benefit has been changed to 50% to 125%. Families of workers who die from work-related accidents should be given survivor benefits. The amount is one-third to three-quarters of the deceased worker's original wage in cities, depending on the number of applicants, and 7 to 47 rubles per month for those working in rural agricultural areas.

In addition, before October 1930, there were subsidies for the unemployed, but these have long been abolished. | November 28

Business News: Financial Foreign Exchange Rate Weakens by Another Point 272

In the morning market, over 4.4 million was transferred, with over 300,000 in new transactions. Securities: The Situation is Depressing - Bond Market Watched Last Week - Sharp Decline in Transactions, Mixed Rise and Fall - 273

Last week, from December 11th to 16th, the Chinese Merchant Securities Market suddenly became stable, and trading also declined significantly. Both bulls and bears were largely holding back and watching, which has been rare in recent years. The situation is depressing, with no new developments. The representatives' negotiations have no concrete solutions, and the biggest disputes have not been effectively resolved. However, war may not break out suddenly, and peace is not yet hopeless. Opinions differ, and both sides have their own views, so the stalemate is intensifying. The end of the year is approaching, and it is unlikely that this stalemate will continue. On Monday, due to rumors that the war clouds in Fujian and Zhejiang were thickening, the bulls emerged, and prices fell by several jiao to about one yuan and a half. On Tuesday, the news was better, and war might be avoided. The bears slightly compensated, and market prices rebounded by several jiao to one yuan and three or four jiao. The one-day decline and one-day rise balanced out. On Wednesday, the situation remained depressing, and large investors made slight purchases, continuing to rise by several jiao. On Thursday, northern merchants slightly sold, and market prices hovered wearily, falling back by a small six or seven jiao. On Friday, due to the postponement of the Fourth Plenary Session, people's hearts were slightly uneasy, and prices fluctuated suddenly, falling slightly by three or four jiao. Although transactions were particularly small on Saturday, market prices rose slightly in each session, with a total increase of six or seven jiao. As a result, market prices showed mixed gains and losses, but the fluctuations were only within three to five jiao. The total transaction volume was 75.157 million yuan. Oil Market: Tallow Oil, Han Market Drops Sharply 278

Tallow oil is supposed to be abundant during the new production season, but sales have actually decreased significantly compared to previous years. The biggest reason for this is the decline of rural areas. Furthermore, the Chen oil in Hankou still has reserves. The market in Hankou has been trending downward from autumn to winter. After the new oil came out, the weak trend has worsened. Macheng oil was able to hold on to around 17 yuan for more than a month, but now with the abundant arrival of new goods, it is even more difficult to maintain. According to yesterday's telegram from Hankou, Macheng oil has already fallen to 16 yuan 3 jiao, and yesterday's telegram showed another drop to 15 yuan 45 jiao. The strength of the price drop is unprecedented in the second half of the year. In addition, the source is connected, and sales are blocked, so there is no possibility of a turnaround in the short term. As for the Zhejiang route, initially, because the Chen oil was selling well, there was a brief period of good sales when the new oil came out. New goods in the areas of Jinhua and Lanxi in eastern Zhejiang were purchased at 16 yuan, and then rose to 17 yuan. In Jiaxing and other places in western Zhejiang, the opening price was 19 yuan, which increased to 21 yuan. Recently, since the Fujian incident occurred, the impact has been felt, and Lanxi tallow has returned to 16 yuan and 15 yuan 78 jiao. The price of japonica oil in Hebei is also falling to 19 yuan 56 jiao. The above are all prices in the production areas. Lanxi is not sold in Shanghai, but the japonica oil from Hebei is needed by candle manufacturers in Shanghai. The current market price for delivery to Shanghai is between 20 yuan and 23 jiao. There have been slight transactions in recent days, but after the sharp drop in the Han market, people inevitably hope for lower prices, so merchants are not enthusiastically purchasing. However, because it is the right time for candle making, the scattered transactions in the market are not too deserted.

White Tung Oil, Zhejiang Route Slightly Firm 279

White tung oil in the Han market has been falling continuously due to sluggish foreign sales. The Zhejiang route is gradually weakening due to the impact of the current situation. The market conditions in both the North and South are trending in the same direction. Yesterday's telegram from foreign merchants in the Han market showed a drop to 22 yuan. Although there were transactions of 100-200 tons, with the abundant production of new goods, the source is quite abundant, and the market is still oversupplied. Domestic sales are also in a slump during the winter season, so it is difficult to expect a turnaround in the short term. Before the Zhejiang tung oil, due to the impact of the Fujian incident, people were understandably panicked in Jinhua and Lanxi in eastern Zhejiang, which are close to the Fujian border. As a result, the price of Lanxi tung oil fell first, and Hangzhou merchants also stopped purchasing. The market price fell to 19 yuan per dan for spot delivery, and transactions also became quiet. However, recently the situation on the Zhejiang border has gradually become more stable, and commercial activity has slightly increased, so the tung oil market has slightly recovered. According to recent news, Hangzhou merchants have sent people to Shanghai to sell oil, and the price is 20 yuan and 2 jiao for delivery to Shanghai, which shows that they seem to be more energetic than a few days ago. Although there are not many transactions, the market conditions are showing signs of activity. It is hoped that the situation will not change again, so the market will not face the risk of further decline. However, the Han market is the center of foreign trade, and since the market has been weak and difficult to revive, the Zhejiang tung oil will inevitably be restrained by it. Although the Zhejiang tung oil can be unique for a while, it must ultimately rely on the Han market.

A FURTHER EXPLANATION FOR IMPOSING INHERITANCE TAX 281

— Non-Person

According to recent telegraphic dispatches, the financial authorities are planning to levy an inheritance tax. The implementation method will soon be realized. In various countries, inheritance tax is originally one of the direct taxes, and it occupies a very important position in national finance. However, no matter how wonderful and good a system is in other countries, if it is implemented in our country, it will be ruined and become sour orange. This is a tried and tested result.

Taking inheritance tax as an example, truly wealthy people would rather pay interest to deposit their money in foreign banks. If they hear that inheritance tax is implemented, depositing money in foreign banks will definitely be more enthusiastic. Those who can be collected from will only be the middle and lower-class asset class. As for those who are particularly powerful and wealthy, national laws inherently cannot reach them. In this way, it will only be a great boon for foreign bankers. As for the country, in reality, it will not gain any benefits. This is an obvious thing.

This point is just a hypothetical prediction that I make based on the inheritance tax system. In fact, when creating a system, on the one hand, it is for the sake of the country, and on the other hand, it is naturally even more for the sake of the people. If the inheritance tax is levied, it is only for the sake of the country and not for the sake of the people. If both sides are to be taken into account and both benefit, then the inheritance system must be abolished. As for the reason, please allow me to slowly explain it after I finish my cigarette.

Too much money is harmful to descendants. History and reality in society have proclaimed this fact to us, and examples are too numerous to mention. As the saying goes, "No outstanding children come from families of silk-clad idlers." The ancients said: "It is better to accumulate virtue for your descendants than to accumulate wealth for them." And: "It is better to teach your children a classic than to accumulate wealth for them." To be honest, accumulating money for descendants is not creating blessings for them, but harming them. The ancients, with their "firefly" bellies, saw this very clearly.

Although what the ancients said is not wrong, it is only thinking of descendants from a one-sided perspective, without thoroughly thinking of oneself. Look at the people in the world today, all are strong, fierce, tyrannical, demanding, mean, ungrateful, exploitative, and greedy, using all means to accumulate hundreds of thousands of fortunes, but they are not satisfied. They must accumulate millions. Accumulating millions is not enough. They still want to accumulate tens of millions, to the point that they want to scrape all the wealth in the world for themselves. Such people who "stretch out their hands from the coffin and still want more" can be said to be everywhere.

I want to ask, among the millions or tens of millions accumulated, how much can they enjoy themselves? As the saying goes, "Empty hands come, empty hands go." Even if you accumulate gold as high as the Big Dipper, you can't transport it to the underworld. In the end, you are just being a beast of burden for your descendants for a lifetime, living a big dream. As for the descendants, they become extravagant and degenerate, or they fight for the inheritance, even breaking up the family, or they may even give the money to mistresses to find lovers. Truly, ill-gotten gains can never be permanently preserved. Therefore, Confucius said: "Acting with self-interest in mind leads to much resentment."

Why do people become corrupt officials? Why do they become traitors? Why do they become unscrupulous merchants? Why do they do everything that harms others and benefits themselves? In a word, it is all for the sake of their descendants. If the inheritance system is abolished, it would be a targeted solution, a fundamental remedy. Therefore, I say that it is more appropriate to abolish the inheritance system than to levy inheritance tax.

SHANGHAI'S GLOOMY SIDE 282

— Wen

The Shanghai that the leisure class, immersed in pleasure, knows is only the superficial side, adorned with "civilization" and "order." What is reflected from this side is only the satisfaction and intoxication in all aspects of clothing, food, housing, transportation, sex, and entertainment, which are exchanged for a "spending money like dirt" lifestyle. For example, the gorgeous dresses of 1934, the large dishes costing twenty or thirty yuan each, the tens or even hundreds of gold spent per day, the hotel rooms equipped with styles from various countries, the luxurious and brisk motor cars, the smooth and trembling thighs and breasts, the radios that can listen to world sound waves, the bright and colorful neon lights, and all the endless pleasures of wine, women, songs and horses are readily available in this "Paris of the East." The only question is: are your gentlemen's purses full?

However, in this Shanghai, which accommodates many British, Chinese, and foreign people, the "high-class Chinese" foreigners with "money to burn" are, after all, an absolute minority. The "lower class," who make up more than ninety percent, and who have fallen into the starvation line and the slave layer, are living a life of dripping blood, sweating, struggling, and waiting for death. Therefore, on every page of the "bright side" of urban life, which is full of gold and extravagance, there is a tragic, serious, and unimaginable gloomy side mixed in. As we see through this contrasting life of heaven and hell, we must not only feel the irrationality of the current urban life, but also think of the terrible fate of the future of the social enjoyment class, which is too small in quantity and too poor in quality.

In the towering buildings of the Cathay Hotel, the Palace Hotel, or the Astor House Hotel, one can overlook the sky and look down on the world. Inside the windows and doors, there is air conditioning and electric fans in the hot summer, and radiators and electric stoves in the winter. Such a place is of course considered a "paradise on earth" in Shanghai life. However, just a few or a dozen feet away outside the window, countless coolies are loading and unloading heavy goods while uttering "Heave-ho" sounds under the "creaking" sound of the cranes on the ships, enduring the scolding or "abuse" of the foremen. At the same time, the "respected arm" of the foremen is often cocked in preparation for accepting "kickbacks." This is just two polar opposite pictures separated by a piece of glass from the life inside the aforementioned hotels!

If someone believes that this huge metropolis lacks "security" and "order" because they see the endless cases of murder, kidnapping, rape, and robbery in Shanghai, then perhaps that is their "mistake." "Order" cannot be sought in factory areas or slums. To see the "order" of Shanghai, you must go to the corner of Carlton and Jing'an Temple Road, the intersection of Avenue Joffre and Avenue Petain, and those places on Avenue Albert to investigate. Whenever the movies end, the Jai Alai and dog racing begin or end, there are extra Chinese and foreign patrol officers stationed there to chase away "idlers," whip rickshaw pullers, and arrange a large number of cars in orderly rows. The Carlton, New Light, or Great Light theaters swallow and spit out thousands of old and young men and women who have a sense of gentility three times a day. Whenever it is 8:30 or 11:00 when the show ends, every corner of the several roads surrounding these three major theaters is filled with loafers who listen to your accent and pretend to be "fellow villagers" to ask for copper coins, and prostitutes who have to go back to "starvation" if they cannot get any "business." The Central Stadium and the Cathay Theatre, a "three-dimensional building," face each other from afar. On Avenue Joffre, which is full of "exotic flavors" and "mysterious scents," in addition to the gambling of the foreign gangsters with "Hail, Hail" and the sensual and erotic movies, there are "massage parlors" that offer "steaming, washing, rubbing, and massaging" all four services for one dollar, and all kinds of Russian secret dens. In that mysterious street, you can always meet Russian loafers who raise their thumbs at you and shout the slogan "Chinese, very good!" in exchange for one or two copper coins. Dear readers! You must remember: these "poor" but deserving Russian men and women were the most adept at extravagance and pleasure-seeking in the era when "the aura of the Tsar had not yet faded" in Petrograd! Beyond the solemn Soochow Road Police Station, the large section west of the Big Bell Tower is the base camp for many "opium dens," and the area around East and West New Bridge and the Great World is even more of a "defense line" with "women soldiers" forcibly pulling or carrying "country bumpkins" every five steps, ten steps a post. All of these "ghosts and monsters" are openly displayed on the roads like harmonious buildings and prosperous commerce. It is completely a human hell, not just the gloomy side of the metropolis!

The Wutong Road near Jing'an Temple and Yuyuan Road is long and slightly unstained, and various villas and alleys are so neat and luxurious, but in the factory area around Caojiadu, countless men and women workers with emaciated faces and calloused hands are constantly breathing air full of coal smoke and living in pigeon cages where "eating, drinking, sleeping, and defecating" are completed in a six-foot square space. Further away, the shantytowns around Sun Temple and Qingyun Road in Zhabei are even using straw and wood chips as building materials and flatbread and fried dough sticks as precious food. If they encounter a disaster where "the heavens do not open their eyes," a fire or a gust of north wind can leave them with nothing, causing death and destruction! However, the number of workers and shantytown dwellers is dozens of times greater than the wealthy people living in spacious mansions and hotels!

A CHAT ABOUT FRIENDSHIP 283

— Burial

丨丨 Presented to Brother Yi Ping 丨丨

Unexpectedly, the "Pained Heart" that I wrote in a panic after my father passed away actually received your sincere comfort! In fact, why is this unexpected? Usually, when I read your essays and novels, every word reveals sincerity! It was two or three months ago, wasn't it, that you published a series of articles describing your friend's illness, writing about how you were concerned and running around for your friend, and writing about how upright your new friend Fei was, all of which made people feel relaxed and refreshed, and made them feel that their wounded lives were washed anew. Even in our brief meeting, the impression you gave me was very deep: straightforward in speech, pure in expression, deep and sharp in your eyes丨丨丨 everything! Precisely because of this, only you can understand the "Pained Heart" of a new friend you had only met once. However, because I am used to seeing the ferocious faces of ordinary people, applying my usual standards, I could not help but be a little surprised when I suddenly saw your words, thinking that it was unexpected. This is, of course, my unprotectable guilt, and it is also the reason why we have so few opportunities to get together.

Because of this, it has stirred up my understanding of friendship. In this society, no matter in which corner, friendship can generally be divided into three types: First, hypocritical friendship, which is pretending a dead face as a living face, and perfunctorily dealing with others with smooth talk; second, friendship of interest, which unites and becomes affectionate when there is benefit, and separates and becomes distant when there is harm. The rise and fall of this friendship is entirely measured by interest. One moment it is as warm as a molten blob of sealing wax, and another it is as incompatible as ice and coal; third, sardonic friendship. In this capitalist society, all forms are originally a sardonic performance, and friendship cannot avoid this model. Many people come and go in sardonic laughter. The defect of these three types of friendship is the lack of "sincerity." It can simply be said that not a trace of sincerity can be found. The bond between each other is all hypocrisy, self-interest, and sardonic laughter. This is a reflection of the hateful real society, and it is also the wound of the entire human life. We cannot feel the invasion of this wound, we need sincere friendship. From a certain social consciousness, so-called sincere friendship seems to be a trivial matter, and there is no need to praise it so much. However, my temperament is just destined to be like this. I deeply feel that human beings are not only rational animals, but also emotional ones. Reason must be nourished by emotion in order for life to be fulfilled and rich. Therefore, I am often afraid of the famine of life, and I eagerly thirst for the irrigation of sincere friendship.

Having lived for twenty-three years, in terms of the strength of friends, I am not considered to have many, but not few either. But many have disappointed me, making me retreat, because they mostly treat me with general friendship. When I approach them, I feel cramped, I feel heartbroken! I want to get rid of these and pursue those. In the past two years, I jumped out of school and climbed into society. Although life has been hitting walls everywhere, I am privately fortunate to have met several sincere friends that I have been longing for in my life. Our interaction has completely broken away from the dead shells of hypocrisy, self-interest, and sardonic laughter. We are all walking hand in hand on the path of sincere friendship. This makes me feel the loveliness of human beings and the worthiness of life. From now on, my life will be entirely promoted by this!

Needless to say, you are another one I long for! You have become a flower in my life! I don't know if you are willing? I am a little timid, because my own resources are very scarce, and my life is too narrow! Precisely because of this, I dare not easily try to find new friends, and that is why I have not met you again or corresponded with you since our "one-sided" meeting. But today, I have deeply recognized you. Perhaps you have the same intentions as me 丨丨 needing a lower-level friend like me. Then, friend, let us walk hand in hand on the path of sincere friendship!

Finally, thank you for your comfort. My hometown does not belong to me. I must return to that place, that is my hometown, and it is not far away. My father has passed away, and I will seek to repay him through the life he left me! At the same time, I advise you, old brother: don't be sad that your father died when you were two years old!

SCOIDING 284

— Yi Ping

Our country claims to be an ancient civilization in the world, so it has done special research on the art of scolding. From the time when children write "XXX is really not good" and "XXX little know-it-all" on other people's black walls, to scolding people as "running dogs" and "traitors"... announcing "ten major crimes," there are numerous classes, too many to list. As for scolding other people's ancestors for eight generations and their reproductive organs, it is even a small matter and not worth mentioning!

Perhaps because my surname has a slightly similar pronunciation to the name of a certain famous writer, I have been scolded as a copycat. Although I wrote a statement, I regretted it afterwards. No matter how I said that the two characters "Yi Ping" have had a relationship with me for twenty-five years, and that the surname Zhang is even inherited from my ancestors and I have not been adopted into another surname, it is something that cannot be helped. But statements are statements, and you will still be scolded. Isn't writing an additional statement just asking for more scolding? However, why are you spending so much energy to tease an unknown person like me? Perhaps it is because of the sins committed by old man Xiao when he came to Shanghai!

This year, I have written a few more "Love Stories" in this publication, and have added the title of petty bourgeois to the head of a poor kid like me who lives in a garret. Originally, those of us who were not born with good fortune cannot obtain the life of the petty bourgeoisie even if we seek it. Writing articles (?) is just to cheat manuscript fees. "Love Stories" are fine, or random nonsense is fine. Filling the manuscript paper, passing through the eyes of the editor, and then being set in lead type by the printer and printed in the newspaper is all that matters. No matter what is written, I don't expect to print any separate editions. A thousand words becomes three dollars, no matter where it comes from! And I am not blessed to receive this malicious compliment of petty bourgeois. I respectfully return it to that gentleman.

Recently, "Shanghai" was published in this publication. The pen name is Lao San. Besides the editor of this publication and my close friends, no third person knows about it. Two weeks ago, I received a letter, which was forwarded from our radio communications office, without a signature. The person who wrote the letter scolded me like scolding someone's ancestors for eight generations. Finally, he asked me why Xu Huiqin in Shanghai was written as such a typical woman. So I became paranoid and thought that the gentleman (?) who wrote the letter was defending my ideal Xu Huiqin. But how can he (?) know that Lao San is my pen name? Of course, it is not out of the scope of the first or second type of people. I asked the editor of this publication, and the answer was that no one came to inquire who Lao San was. But my close friends, I believe that there is no such boring person who would deliberately change his handwriting, bury his name, and play such a joke on me. I hope that the gentleman (?) who wrote the letter will give me a chance to meet. I want to personally ask for advice, or it may make the gentleman (?) feel more comfortable. I don't know what the gentleman (,) thinks?

MY FRIEND 285

— Bei

My friend is not Hu Shih, but Man, who is imprisoned in prison.

On the eve of the "January 28th Incident," we had met and talked about the current affairs. After the Japanese soldiers casually attacked one night, we all fell into the abyss of terror, and the connection of meetings was cut off in a few days. One day I met Long on the road, and he said urgently: "Man has found a connection, and he has a letter for you." At that time, I really found it strange and strange. The timing was so terrifying, and he was such an arrogant character, how could he find a connection? I couldn't help but blurt out "Don't talk nonsense!" "You're right, this is the letter he asked me to give you, see what's written inside?" Long said seriously, and at the same time took out Man's crookedly written leaf of letter paper and handed it to me:

"Friend, I didn't expect that after not seeing each other for a few days, we are separated by a world! On the night of the 30th, I originally planned to squeeze in to sleep at Fan Na'er's, but several of his female relatives escaped and came over, so I had no choice but to think of another way: I walked out, and just as I reached the corner of □□□ Road □□□ Road, I was stopped by two police officers, who ordered me to stop. Then they searched my body extensively, even grabbed a few times under my crotch. As a result, they found my diary and several letters from friends that were completely unrelated in the pocket of my undershirt next to my skin. So they said that during this martial law period, I was quite suspicious, and took me to the police station, and then to the court, and without any explanation, they sentenced me to five years in prison for endangering the Republic of China. Friend, you should think of a way for me!"

"Ah, so that's how it is, injustice, injustice, it's really injustice 丨 but it is indeed a temporary connection!" Only then did I understand Long's meaning, and I added a word of praise to Man's unjust encounter in the same tone.

"Really, don't talk nonsense anymore, it's not fun after all. Let's find a lawyer to appeal for him!" Long became anxious, so we went to find a former teacher together. The teacher introduced us to a lawyer. After we explained the facts, the lawyer repeatedly shook his head and asked: "Is his family well-off?" "Not very good!" The lawyer shook his head again and said: "Then it's difficult! It's a political prisoner! Political prisoners have no money..." The rest was a smile with a frown. After talking left and right, we finally agreed to trouble him for one hundred yuan, and the lawyer agreed hesitantly: "I can only not count so much." This made us extremely excited, as if Man was standing right in front of us. So we wrote a letter to Man's house, saying that he was very ill and needed to find a way to send one hundred yuan to treat him.

Man wanted me to see him, God knows. I went at nine o'clock in the morning, and waited until half past twelve before we were allowed to meet each other through a small iron fence opening the size of a vegetable bowl. We could not see his face, and could only listen to his voice carefully. Man said: "Bei, it's you who came. First I tell you, the cashier of the detention center took five yuan of my oil. Please go and negotiate for me!..." The supervising bailiff became furious: "The prisoner still doesn't follow the rules, scolding people casually, cancel the visit!" "XXX your mother, XXX your mother!" Man scolded even more fiercely in the prison. The limited five minutes passed by in a hurry, so we can say that we didn't talk about anything at all.

Coming out, I was very angry and went to find the cashier of the detention center, but they ignored me.

After that, a long time passed without the money being sent. I was also busy with my life, so I only sent him some food and newspapers. It was not until last winter that I got another letter from him. He said: "The appeal has been ruled again, still five years, and the five yuan is still being used to buy old oil. Only a bottle of chili oil was received from some food, and the newspapers and magazines were not delivered at all." From this, we can regret that the one hundred yuan lawyer's appeal fee was just like throwing it into the river, without even a bubble rising. The latest news from Man made me very excited. He said that he would no longer fight any laws with those dogs, and he did not want to appeal for injustice or dream of any commutation of sentence or amnesty for the time being. He is now concentrating on studying, preparing for the real struggle in the future. He has mastered a foreign language, and is proficient in French.

Yes, Man, this is the appropriate treatment for you! As long as you have a life, you will have the tools to fight. The short five years have passed, and the world is still yours! Although you have suffered injustice this time, it is the beginning of your true life! At present, this world is originally a huge prison, friend, be patient! Work hard! Lay the foundation for you to reverse the era after you are released from prison! (The End)

NOVEL

SHANGHAI (21) 286

— Zhang Lao San

"Hmm?" Gao Fei suddenly stopped.

"What?"

"You don't know?"

"Who knows!"

"It's all Min's money! Our friends can help you a lot!"

"Hmm." We continued to walk forward, dragging long shadows on the road. The autumn wind was blowing the leaves on the roadside, and autumn had unknowingly embarked on its journey.

(32) Thank You

I can't believe that a vagrant who escaped from his stepmother is immersed in the embrace of two different types of women. I remember dreaming of my father, that serious face, that serious voice. Although I have not left my younger brother, how can this kind of life be what I hoped for when I left my hometown? Two months of entanglements on the bed have been my undeniable fact. "You have been surrounded by women!" The voice of that serious father is forever remembered in my heart.

One clear morning, I received a letter from my cousin, sent by someone. My uncle's matter required me to go to Xujiahui. I seemed very ashamed. I have been in Shanghai for almost a year, and the old cotton robe on my body is even more tattered. If the doorman always puts on a face of a superior seeing a subordinate, it would be very good. I am really afraid of seeing the humble young master who is in every way higher than me in formality; but this may be the opportunity for us young people that my cousin said. If I want to escape the surrounding reality, I must first get rid of the cage of the Zhengyi Society.

Finally, I arrived at the iron gate of Fangwai Villa like a thief. As if he was waiting for me, the doorman's head was already smiling in front of me before I raised my hand to press the doorbell. However, the loud voice of "young master" was replaced by his sneaky words. As I stepped sideways through the iron gate, he leaned slightly and said by my side:

"Young master, please go to the living room first, Miss is waiting."

I glanced at him, and he went back to the guard room with a smiling face. With a ghost in my heart, after walking through the stone-paved path, my cousin jumped out at the door of the Western-style house, like a cute kitten. She took my hand and walked into the living room, with the first sentence: "Sit for a while, father has not gotten up yet."

"Is that the reason?"

"No!" A cigarette came with a charming smile "Dad recently made a deal and earned tens of thousands. He is happy every day. He promised me to buy a ring. I said that you have been in Shanghai for almost a year, and you are still living in a friend's house. You had a serious illness the other day. Let Dad arrange a seat for him."

"Thank you." I feel that there is nothing to be surprised about.

"Who wants you to thank you!" Sister Hui stamped her leather shoes on the floor with a strange sound "I want to tell you first, don't let the two people's words say different things." A kind of satisfied smile cannot be concealed no matter what.

"Then I have to thank you even more!"

"Don't be so long-winded, let's go see Dad."

"Uncle hasn't gotten up yet?"

"He should be up." Sister Hui looked at the clock on the wall, "Isn't it eleven o'clock?"

I looked at her face and felt that this time I came to Fangwai Villa was escaping from one cage and entering another.

MOVIE SPECIAL

An Interview with Chinese Film Artists (28) (Continued from the 6th of this Month) 287

— Sha Ji

12. "New Year's Eve" Director Jiang Qifeng (Part 1)

I remember when "New Year's Eve" premiered at the Beijing Grand Theater, everyone was amazed by it. Not only were some of the shots beautifully composed, but the structure of the story, being able to create a film of around 10,000 feet in such a short period, was truly not easy. Similar examples include "Grand Hotel" or the British "Rome Express," and the upcoming MGM's "Dinner at Eight." The Star Motion Picture Company's "Twenty-Four Hours" (directed by Shen Xiling) is also like this…

"New Year's Eve" is unforgettable. Therefore, I went to Lianhua Studio One to interview the creator. In a small reception room, we each had a cup of strong tea in front of us. We smoked, and white smoke clouds swirled above our heads. The yellow chrysanthemums in the corner had already withered, hiding in the dark corner, afraid to move. Pale gray light poured down from the skylight in the roof, making me feel the solemnity of the air.

Mr. Jiang was wearing a cotton robe made of genuine domestic fabric, and on his feet were just eight-cornered cloth shoes. His simple demeanor moved me at first. After I stated my purpose, he was full of humility. He first explained that he could not speak "Mandarin," so I occasionally spoke with him in a Shanghai accent.

Our conversation was in a question-and-answer format. I said, "Mr. Jiang, what are your opinions on the current state of Chinese cinema?"

"In my personal opinion, although Chinese cinema has changed, it is still very empty. In this regard, Chinese film practitioners need the practical assistance of critics. That is to say, to revitalize Chinese cinema, critics must urge and encourage the creators. This is because the bystander sees the game, but the player is blind..."

"However, in fact, we are now facing what seems to be a serious period, and some writers inevitably want to regress. What attitude does Mr. Jiang take?"

"That's hard to say... Perhaps my will is very weak... However, I always firmly believe that movies cannot be separated from the masses. We must always make things that are needed by the public. Anything that the public needs, we must boldly do."

In his smiling humility, he vaguely revealed a firm attitude. Afterwards, I asked again, "Please say something about your own works."

"Well, to be honest, I am not satisfied with any of my own works. Counting it up, I have been in the film industry for ten years, but I have made no progress. At the beginning, I was at the Great China-United Film Company. Later, I was delayed in various small companies for a long time. But the environment of small companies is not good, and I was ruined in such a bad environment. After arriving at Lianhua, there is comparatively more room for development."

"What are your opinions on 'New Year's Eve'?"

"'New Year's Eve' has a complicated plot, and its significance is not sound. However, I had a lot of bitterness in filming this film. The director suffered a lot and lost a lot. At that time, because everyone was not filming, and I just happened to have no script." (To be continued)

Film Review

Review of "Love in the Wilds" 288

— Ling He

Ladies They Talk About

| Warner Bros. Production, Cathay Screening |

Impressionistic criticism is certainly dissatisfying to readers, and the friends who write such criticisms—at least myself—always feel very distressed. Criticizing literature or drama is the same. Before starting to criticize, one must fully grasp the entire work before beginning to write out one's opinions in a relatively in-depth way. However, current film critics do not have this possibility. After watching it once, they must hurriedly write articles. No matter how sensitive a person is, they cannot write a perfectly complete critique. This does indeed make me feel very uneasy. I hope that friends in the same field can come up with a better way to solve this difficulty.

For example, in this "Love in the Wilds," I can only write out a few very simple opinions based on my impressions.

(1) The author tries to beautify the prison as much as possible, which is most inconsistent with the life emotions of the Chinese people. There are gardens and beautiful smoking rooms in the prison. Female prisoners each have an exquisite room. They play phonographs, sing, play the piano, and hang photos of their lovers on the walls. This is definitely not a prison, but a nursing home. I think some of the readers may be willing to live there for a year or two.

However, the author has intentions. This is linked to the theme of using the Bible and love to influence criminals. The beautification of the prison is an important refutation. Originally, the author did not need to bother to describe it.

(2) Praising the merits of Protestantism is the main content of the work. But do we see that the heroine's female thief is completely influenced by the religion? Rather than saying that the power of God has influenced the soul of the criminal, it is more accurate to say that the Protestant working in the court softened her with his enthusiasm.

(3) However, exaggerating love so much is also unbelievable. For example, the female criminal shoots her lover, but the injured person can bear the pain to defend her without any resentment.

Moreover, the personality of the male protagonist is also very contradictory. On the one hand, we see him being impassioned and generous, seemingly an amazing hero. But he is so gentle and obedient to the female prisoner, especially since the woman has nothing lovable about her. The screenwriter's explanation is that she possesses superhuman magic.

(4) The director's greatest success is clearly and understandably narrating the story. However, there are several well-controlled scenes. The fun and quirky gimmicks are the forte of American artists.

(5) The playwright's imagination is indeed rich. Such as printing a key model on soap, looking at letters in the laundry box, and pre-arranging the bank robbery. Are these useful lessons for society?

Well, all I can write is these impressions, nothing more.

Review of "New Woman" 289

— Moore

Lady With A Past

"New Woman" followed "Modern Don Quixote" in being screened in Nanjing. "Modern Don Quixote" was adapted by experts based on a "famous work of world literature, and it gathered first-class talents in film and vocal music for production. Its result was so tragic (only showing for four days) that I cannot help but lament the monopolization of artistic appreciation, and I feel even more strongly the need for truly popular film productions. On the one hand, because of the box-office success of the films starring Heifetz about male and female affairs, I feel the weakness of the effect of new film criticism. Furthermore, I feel that attention should be paid to the criticism of the form determined by the consciousness and content of the film. I am deeply worried about the danger of new critics being fascinated by the old forms (such as praise for having interest in the old forms.)"

The translated title "New Woman" is very inconsistent with its original meaning. "Lady with a Past" was originally a stage play, but now it has been brought to the screen and presented in a comedic way.

Recently, after the close attention of many friends, American films have gradually abandoned purely fantasy themes and have returned to social reality. (Warner Bros.' attention to exposing films, which caused a sensation for a while, is clear evidence of this.) "New Woman" is undoubtedly a relatively realistic film. Of course, the story is still about male and female love, but it is no longer about talented men and beautiful women falling in love at first sight. It writes about how a rich girl goes from being silent in nature to having extensive social interactions, being romantic and frivolous: there is a certain inevitable relationship in the middle, or at least conditions. It writes about how a handsome young man does not dare to offend a dignified and self-respecting girl, but is infatuated with a enchanting and romantic prostitute. It writes about how viscounts pursue women because "Fan (the heroine) is rich, and they think marrying her can lead to wealth," thus exposing the face of the doctrine of love above all else. Not only that, it also adds bankruptcy to the viscount's suicide, in addition to being lovelorn, so that his suicide does not make the audience feel impossible or unrealistic. The best thing is that it writes about the young man and Donna, who he had not paid much attention to, coming together after a series of personal storms and a new awakening. This is where the screenwriter succeeds.

As for the director, I think the most successful thing is the inner description of the girl and the boy. The confusion and contradiction when the boy loves the girl but does not dare to court her, the hesitation when the enchanting prostitute seduces him, and the fact that he knows the prostitute's character but is involuntarily captivated by her beauty; all of these are perfectly portrayed. As for the girl's inner distress when she first falls in love, as well as her progress after experiencing a period of time, and her final hesitation, it can be said that there is no place that is not reasonable and in line with human emotions. This is of course due to their (including all producers) life experiences, and this is also the reason why this film ultimately became an old art, and its value is limited in this place.

Under the director's guidance, the performances of the male and female leads achieved everything that was needed without any regrets.

Film Industry Sports: Yi Hua vs. Great China University 290

— Bi Mei

The last time Yi Hua Company competed in football against Jiaotong University and Lianhua Company, they fought dozens of rounds. If Yue Feng, the goalkeeper for Yi Hua, had worked a little harder, Lianhua would have been defeated! However, although the two sides did not see victory or defeat, Yi Hua's football skills earned them the nickname "Iron Army" in the film industry.

After Jin Yan and Gong Jianong launched the film industry track and field competition, the Yi Hua Iron Army suddenly felt that they had no place to use their heroism. However, several athletes did not slack off because of this, and they continued to practice hard during their spare time after meals.

Sure enough, the news spread and excited the academic community. The day before yesterday (14th), the "Roaring Basketball Team" of Great China University, led by nearly ten brave generals and many cheerleaders, went to the Yi Hua Company's sports field to compete in basketball. At that time, Yi Hua carefully selected their elites, and they obtained "Zha Ruilong, Hu Rui, Zha Ruigen, Wang Chunquan, and Yao Gengfu" to compete against them.

At exactly 3:20, the Yi Hua sports field was filled with war cries. The two armies fought hard five times. The generals of Great China University were all familiar with the ropes and dealt with each other from all sides. However, Zha Ruigen of Yi Hua Company worked very hard. Once he had the ball in hand, it was as if it was tied with a string. Every shot went in, and he jumped extremely high. As a result, Great China University scored 33 points, and Yi Hua scored 38 points. Great China University lost by 5 points. It was already dusk, so they each withdrew their troops. (Rewarding)

The Play-within-a-Play in "A Movie Star" 291

"A Movie Star," which has been promoted for a long time, was completely completed a few days ago. About four days ago, the Tianyi photography studio was bustling with activity, re-shooting a play-within-a-play scene. In this scene, we can see the actual work in the photography studio, male and female protagonists, extras, directors, cinematographers, script supervisors, and all the workers, as well as… things we rarely see, are all exposed here. Many people envy the life of a movie star, thinking that it is a very interesting and meaningful job, and they all want to step into the silver sea to try it out. It would even be good to go to the photography studio to take a look. Wait, don't miss this "A Movie Star."

Film Novel Little Women (13) 292

— Su Yin

Qiao wordlessly picked her up, held her close to her heart, and carried her into the house. Mother March brought a cup of soup, followed by Father and Meg. Beth looked at them and smiled slightly. "I want to sleep for a while," she said. Qiao then straightened the cushion under her body and gently put her down. Beth's eyes searched for the light from the window, and a smile appeared in her eyes. "Look," she said, "my birds have just come back." Her head tilted back, and her eyes slowly closed. Qiao cried, "Beth," and called out to Mother March. Meg hugged her father and cried as well.

When Laurie heard the sound of mourning from the March family in Europe, he immediately traveled thousands of miles to Switzerland to find Amy. Amy cried in Laurie's arms. Laurie comforted her, saying that he would not leave her until the wounds in her heart had healed. So he came to accompany Amy to play every day. One day, they were rowing a boat on the lake, and Laurie suddenly stared at her without blinking. How beautiful she was! She had grown up. The coquettish affectations of her childhood had now turned into natural manners. Her golden hair hung beside her rosy cheeks, truly charming, and the sorrows she had suffered over the years had made her character more dignified and solemn. Laurie silently looked at her, and suddenly felt his heart beating as if it had never beaten like that before.

Amy felt his gaze on her. She said, "You must be tired. Let me row for you." Laurie seemed to wake up from a dream and quickly said, "I'm not tired, but if you want to row, we can row together." As dusk fell, a boat rowed slowly far away on the lake, and two dark shadows swayed on the surface of the lake. "Aren't we rowing well?" Amy finally broke the long silence. Laurie said, "Extremely well. I wish we could always be in the same boat, passing the leisurely years together." He put down the oars and softly asked, "Is that okay, Amy?" Amy frowned and said, "But Laurie, haven't you and Qiao always loved each other?" Laurie said, "Yes. I still love her very much. But the love is different now. Amy, that kind of love is childish and cannot last. Qiao used to try to make me understand, but I didn't want to listen to her, and I even got angry at her because of her. But Qiao was right. Amy, things are different now. I am an adult now. You are my sunlight, and I hope you can always shine on me. Amy, is that okay?" Amy's voice was so low that it could not be heard, but there were a few very clear words: "Yes, Laurie." (To be continued)
